Ruzi qijomat tarozuhoi adlro omoda mekunem va ʙa hec kas sitam namesavad. Agar amale ʙa sanginii jak xardal ham ʙosad, ʙa hisoʙas meovarem, ki mo hisoʙ kardanro ʙasandaem
Ba Muso va Horun kitoʙe dodem, ki haqqu ʙotilro az jakdigar cudo mekunad va ravsanivu pand ast ʙaroi parhezgoron
Onon, ki az Xudoi xud dar nihon metarsand va az ruzi qijomat harosnokand
In muʙorak Qur'onest, ki nozil kardaem, Ojo munkiri on hasted
Pes az in ʙa Iʙrohim quvvai sinoxtasro ato kardem va ʙa u ogoh ʙudem
On goh, ki ʙa padaras va qavmas guft: «In suratho, ki ʙa parastisi onho dil nihodaed, cistand?»
Guftand: «Padaronamonro didem, ki onhoro meparastidand»
Guft: «Alʙatta sumo va padaronaton dar gumrohii oskoro ʙudaed»
Guftand: «Baroi mo suxani haqqe ovardai jo moro ʙa ʙozi giriftai?»
Guft: «Na, Parvardigori sumo Parvardigori osmonhovu zamin ast. On ki onhoro ʙiofaridaast. Va man ʙar in suxan, ki megujam, guvohi mediham
Va ʙa Xudo savgand, ki cun sumo ʙiraved, corai in ʙutonatonro xoham kard»
Onhoro pora-pora kard. Lekin ʙuzurgtarinasonro, pora nakard, sojad ʙar on ruj orand
Guftand: «Ci kas ʙa xudojoni mo cunin kardaast? Alʙatta u az sitamkoron ast!»
Guftand: «Sunidaem, ki cavone ʙa nomi Iʙrohim az onho suxan meguftaast»
Guftand: «Uro ʙa nazdi mardum ʙijovared to sohidi dihand»
Guftand: «Ej Iʙrohim tu ʙo xudojoni mo cunin kardai?»
Guft: «Balki ʙuzurgtarinason cunin kardaast. Agar suxan megujand, az onho ʙipursed»
Bo xudason guftugu kardand va guftand: «Sumo xud sitamkor hasted»
On goh ʙa hajrat sar furu dostand va guftand: «Tu xud medoni, ki inho suxan namegujand»
Guft: «Ojo ƣajri Olloh cizero meparasted, ki na sumoro foida merasonad, na zijon
Bezoram az sumo va az on cizhoe, ki ƣajri Olloh meparasted. Ojo ʙa aql darnamejoʙed
Guftand; «Agar mexohed kore ʙikuned, (Iʙrohimro) ʙisuzoned va xudojoni xudro jori dixed»
Guftem: «Ej otas, ʙar Iʙrohim xunuk va salomat ʙos!»
Mexostand ʙaroi Iʙrohim makre ʙijandesand, vale mo zijonkorason gardonidem
U va Lutro nacot dodem va ʙa sarzamine, ki onro ʙarakati cahonijon qaror dodaem, ʙurdem
Va ʙa u Ishoq va farzandzodae cun Ja'quʙro ʙaxsidem. Va hamaro az soistagon gardonidem
Va hamaro pesvojone soxtem, ki ʙa amri Mo hidojat mekardand. Va ancom dodani korhoi nek va ʙarpoj dostani namoz va dodani zakotro ʙa onho vahj kardem va hama parastandai Mo ʙudand
Va ʙa Lut hukmu ilm dodem va az on deha, ki mardumas korhoi palid mekardand, nacotas ʙaxsidem. Onho, ki mardume ʙadu fosiq ʙudand
Uro dar rahmati xud doxil kardem, ki u az soistagon ʙud
Va Nuhro jod kun, ki pes az on Moro nido dod va Mo ʙa u posux dodem va uvu xonadonasro az mehnate ʙuzurg rahonidem
Va uro ʙar mardume, ki ojoti Moro duruƣ meʙarovardand, piruzi dodem. Onon ʙad mardume ʙudand va Mo hamaro ƣarq soxtem
Va Dovudu Sulajmonro jod kun, on goh ki dar ʙorai kistzore dovari kardand, ki gusfandoni on qavm saʙona dar on co mecaridand. Va Mo sohidi dovarii onho ʙudem
Va in sevai dovariro ʙa Sulajmon omuxtem va hamaro hukmu ilm dodem va kuhhoro mute'i Dovud gardonidem, ki onho va parrandagon ʙo u tasʙeh meguftand va in hama Mo kardem
Va ʙa U omuxtem, to ʙarojaton zireh ʙisozad. To sumoro ʙa hangomi cangidanaton hifz kunad. Ojo siposguzori mekuned
Va tundʙodro farmonʙardori Sulajmon kardem, ki ʙa amri u dar on sarzamin, ki ʙarakatas doda ʙudem, harakat mekard. Va Mo ʙar har cize donoem
Va guruhe az devon ʙarojas dar darjo sinovari mekardand va ƣajri on ʙa korhoi digar masƣul ʙudand va Mo hofizi onho ʙudem
Va Ajjuʙro jod kun, on goh, ki Parvardigorasro nido dod: «Ba man ʙemori va ranc rasidaast va Tu mehruʙontarini mehruʙononi»
Du'ojasro icoʙat kardem. Va ozor az u dur kardem va xonadonasro va monandi onhoro ʙo onho ʙa u ʙozgardonidem. Va in rahmate ʙud az coniʙi Mo to xudoparaston hamesa ʙa jod dosta ʙosand
Va Ismoil va Idris va Zulkiflro jod kun, ki hama az soʙiron ʙudand
Ononro sazovori ʙaxsoisi xud gardonidem va hama az soistagon ʙudand
Va Zunnunro on goh, ki xasmnok ʙiraft va pindost, ki hargiz ʙar u tang namegirem. Va dar toriki nido dod: «X, ec xudoe cuz Tu nest. Tu pok xastj va man az sitamkoron xastam»
Du'ojasro mustacoʙ kardem va uro az andux raxonidem va mu'minonro incunin meraxonem
Va Zakarijoro jod kun, on gox ki Parvardigorasro nido dod: «Ej Parvardigori man, maro tanho vomaguzor. Va Tu ʙehtarini vorisoni!»
Du'ojasro mustacoʙ kardem va ʙa u Jahjoro ʙaxsidem va zanasro ʙarojas soista gardonidem. Inho dar korhoi nek sitoʙ mekardand va ʙa ʙimu umed Moro mexondand va dar ʙaroʙari Mo furutan (sarxam) ʙudand
Va on zanro jod kun, ki sarmgohi xudro nigoh dost va Mo az ruhi Xudo dar u damidem va uvu farzandasro ʙaroi cahonijon iʙrate gardonidem
In sari'ati sumost, sari'ate jagona. Va Man Parvardigori sumojam, Maro ʙiparasted
Va dar dini xud firqa-firqa sudand. Hama ʙa nazdi Mo ʙozmegardand
Har kas, ki kore soista kunad va imon ovarda ʙosad, kusisi uro nosukri nest va Mo amalhojasonro menavisem
Va dehaero, ki ʙa halokat rasonidaem, muhol ast, ki ʙozgaste dosta ʙosand
To on goh, ki Ja'cucu Ma'cuc kusoda savand va onon az ʙalandiho ʙa sitoʙ farojand
Va on va'dai rostin nazdik gardad va casmoni kofiron hamcunon xira monad: «Voj ʙar mo, mo az in hol ƣofil ʙudem. Balki sitamkor ʙudem!»
Sumo va on cizhoe, ki ƣajri Olloh meparastided, hezumhoi duzax hasted. Sumo ʙa duzax xohed raft
Agar inho xudojon meʙudand, ʙa cahannam nameraftand va hol on ki hama dar cahannam covidonand
Onon dar cahannam farjod mekasand va dar on co hec namesunavand
Kasone, ki pes az in muqarrar kardaem, ki ʙa onho nekui kunem, az duzax ʙarkanorand
Inho sadoi duzaxro namesunavand va dar ʙihist, ki har ci xohand, muhajjost, covidonaand
On vahsati ʙuzurg ƣamginason nakunad va faristagon ʙa didorason ojand, ki in hamon ruzest, ki ʙa sumo va'da doda ʙudand
Ruze, ki osmonro cun tumore navista dar ham peconem. Va cunon ki naxustin ʙor ʙijofaridem, ofarinis az sar girem. In va'daest, ki ʙarovardanas ʙar uxdai Most va Mo cunon xohem kard
Va Mo dar Zaʙur, pas az Tavrot, navistaem, ki in zaminro ʙandagoni solehi Man ʙa meros xohand ʙurd
Va dar in kitoʙ taʙliƣest ʙaroi mardumi xudoparast
Va firistodem turo faqat ʙaroi on, ki mexostem ʙa mardumi cahon rahmate ato kunem
Bigu: «Ba man vahj suda, ki Xudoj sumo Xudoest jakto, ojo ʙa U gardan menihed?»
Pas agar rujgardon sudand, ʙigu: «Sumoro xaʙar dodam, to hama dar ogohi jakson ʙosed. Va man namedonam, on ci sumoro va'da kardaand, nazdik ast jo dur
Ust, ki medonad har suxanero, ki ʙa ovozi ʙaland gued jo dar dil pinhon dored
Va namedonam sojad in (der kardani azoʙ) ozmoise ʙaroi sumo va ʙahramandi to ʙa hangomi marg ʙosad»
Guft: «Ej Parvardigori man, ʙa haq dovari kun. Va Parvardigori mo ʙaxsojanda ast va ʙo vucudi on ci megued, hama az U jori mecujand»
Ej mardum, az Parvardigoraton ʙitarsed, ki zilzilai qijomat hodisai ʙuzurgest
On ruz, ki ʙuʙinedas, har sirdihande sirxoraasro az jod ʙiʙarad va har homilae ʙori xudro, ʙar zamin guzorad va mardumro cun maston ʙini, hol on ki mast nestand, ʙalki azoʙi Xudo saxt ast
Ba'ze az mardum ʙe hec donise dar ʙorai Xudo ʙahs mekunand va ʙa dar sajtoni sarkase pajravi mekunand
Bar sajton cunin muqarrar suda, ki har kasro, ki dustas ʙidorad, gumroh kunad va ʙa azoʙi otasi suzonas kasonad
Ej mardum, agar az ruzi qijomat dar suʙha hasted, Mo sumoro az xok va sipas az nutfa, on goh az laxtai xune va sipas az poraguste goh tamom ofarida, goh notamom ʙijofaridaem, to qudrati xudro ʙarojaton oskor kunem. Va to zamone mu'ajjan har ciro xohem, dar rahmxho nigah medorem. On goh sumoro, ki kudake hasted, ʙerun meovarem, to ʙa haddi zurmandii xud rased. Ba'ze az sumo memirandva ʙa'ze ʙa solxurdagi ʙurda mesavand, to on goh ki har ci omuxtaand, faromus kunand. Va tu zaminro xuskida meʙini. Cun ʙoron ʙar on ʙifiris- tem, dar cunʙis ojad va nas'u namo kunad va az har guna gijohi ʙoravnaq ʙirujonad
Va inho dalel ʙar on ast, ki Xudo haq ast, murdagonro zinda mesozad va ʙar har kore tavonost
Va niz qijomat xohad omad, sake dar on nest. Va Xudo hamai kasonero, ki dar gurho hastand, zinda mekunad
Az mardum kasest, ki ʙe hec donise va hec rohnamoi va hec kitoʙi ravsaniʙaxse dar ʙorai Xudo ʙahs mekunad
Gardanro ʙa takaʙʙur ʙa jak su mepeconad, to mardumro az rohi Xudo gumroh sozad. Nasiʙi u dar dunjo xorist va dar ruzi qijomat azoʙi otasro ʙa u mecasonem
In cazoi korhoest, ki pes az in kardai va Xudo ʙa ʙandagonas sitam namekunad
Va az mijoni mardum kasest, ki Xudoro ʙo suʙha meparastad. Agar xajre ʙa u rasad, dilas ʙa on orom girad va agar ozmoise pes ojad, ruj ʙartoʙad. Dar dunjovu oxirat zijon ʙinad va on zijone oskor ast
Ƣajri Xudo kasero mexonad, ki na zijone ʙa u merasonad va na naf'e va in gumrohiest ʙeoxir
Kasero mexonad, ki zijonas nazdiktar az naf'i ust. Ci ʙad dustdorest va ci ʙad hamsuhʙat
Xudo kasonero, ki imon ovarda va korhoi soista kardaand, ʙa ʙihisthoe, ki dar on nahrho corist, doxil mesozad va Xudo har ci xohad, hamon mekunad
Kase, ki mepindorad, ki Xudo dar dunjovu oxirat jorias naxohad kard, xudasro ʙo resmone ʙa saqf ʙijovezad to xudro xafa kunad va ʙingarad, ki ojo in hila xasmasro az mijon xohad ʙurd
Ba in tarz Qur'onro nozil kardem ʙo ojote ravsangar. Va Xudo har kasro, ki ʙixohad, hidojat mekunad
Xudo mijoni onon, ki imon ovardaand va onon, ki dini jahud jo soʙion jo nasoro jo macus ixtijor kardaand va onon, ki musrik sudaand, dar ruzi qijomat hukm mekunad. Zero U ʙar dar kore sohid ast
Ojo nadidai, ki har kas dar osmonhovu har kas, ki dar zamin ast va oftoʙu moh va sitoragonu kuhho va daraxtonu cunʙandagon va ʙisjore az mardum Xudoro sacda mekunand? Va ʙar ʙisjore azoʙ muqarrar suda va har kiro Xudo xor sozad, hec kas giromias namedorad. Zero Xudo har ci ʙixohad, hamon mekunad. (Sacda)
In du guruh dar ʙorai Parvardigorason ʙa xusumat ʙarxostaand. Baroi onon, ki kofirand, comahoe az otas ʙuridaand va az ʙolo ʙar sarason oʙi cuson merezand
Bo on oʙi cuson har ci dar daruni sikam dorand va niz pusthojason gudoxta mesavad
Va niz ʙaroi onhost gurzhoe ohanin
Har goh, ki xohand, az on azoʙ, az on anduh ʙerun ojand, ʙori digar ononro ʙa on ʙozgardonand, ki ʙicased azoʙi otasi suzandaro
Xudo kasonero, ki imon ovarda va korhoi soista kardaand, ʙa ʙihisthoe, ki dar on nahrho corist, doxil mesozad. Dar on co ʙo dastʙandhoe az tillovu marvorid orosta savand va liʙosason az harir ast
Onho ʙa on suxani pok va ʙa rohi Xudovandi sutudani rohnamoi sudaand
Onhoe, ki kofir sudand va mardumro az rohi Xudo va mascidulharom, ki ʙaroi mardumi ci muqimu ci ƣariʙ jakson ast, ʙozmedorand va niz har kiro dar on co qasdi kacravi jo sitamkori dosta ʙosad, azoʙi dardovar mecasonem
Va makoni xonaro ʙaroi Iʙrohim oskor kardem va guftem: «Hec cizro sariki Man masoz va xonai Maro ʙaroi tavofkunandagon va ʙa namoz istodagon va roke'onu socidon pokiza ʙidor»
Va mardumro ʙa hac da'vat kun to pijoda jo savor ʙar suturoni loƣar az rohhoi dur nazdi tu ʙijojand
To naf'hoero, ki az oni onhost, ʙuʙinand va nomi Xudoro dar ruzhoe mu'ajjan ʙa hangomi zaʙhi corpojone, ki Xudo rizqi onho soxta, jod kunand. Pas az onho ʙixuredu ʙenavojoni faqirro niz ta'om dihed
Sipas cirk az xud dur kunand va nazrhoi xudro ado kunand va ʙar on xonai kuhansol tavof kunand
Hamcunin har kas dast az harom ʙidorad, dar nazdi Parvardigoras ʙarojas ʙehtar ast. Va corpojon ʙar sumo haloland, ƣajri onhoe, ki ʙarojaton xonda suda. Pas az ʙuthoi palidu suxani ʙotilu duruƣ parhez kuned
Rujovardagon ʙa Xudo ʙosed va sirknajovardagon ʙa U; va har kas, ki ʙa Xudo sirk ovarad, cun on kasest, ki az osmon furu aftad va murƣ uro ʙiraʙojad jo ʙodas ʙa makone dur andozad
Ore, kasone, ki si'orhoi Xudoro ʙuzurg mesumorand, korason nisoni parhezgorii dilhojason ʙosad
Az on suturoni qurʙoni to zamone mu'ajjan ʙarojaton sudhost, sipas coi qurʙoniason dar on xokai kuhansol ast
Baroi har ummate rasmi qurʙoni kardane nihodem, to ʙa on saʙaʙ, ki Xudo az corpojon ruziason dodaast, nomi Uro ʙar zaʙon ronand. Pas Xudoi sumo Xudoi jaktost, dar ʙaroʙari U taslim saved. Va iʙodatkunandagonro xusxaʙar deh
onon, ki cun nomi Xudo ʙurda savad, dar dil ʙitarsand va ʙa on hangom, ki ʙa onho musiʙate rasad, soʙirand va namozguzoronand va az on ci ruziason dodaem, sadaqa mekunand
Suturoni qurʙoniro ʙaroi sumo az siorhoi Xudo qaror dodem. Sumoro dar on xajrest. Va hamcunon ki ʙar poj istodaand, nomi Xudoro ʙar onho ʙixoned va cun pahlujason ʙar zamin rasid, az onho ʙixured va faqironro qone'u gadojonro ta'om dihed. Inhoro ʙaroi sumo rom kardem. Bosad, ki sukrguzori kuned
Gustu xuni in suturon ʙa Xudo namerasad. On ci ʙa U merasad, parhezgorii sumost. Hamcunin onhoro romi sumo soxt to Xudoro ʙa sukronai on, ki hidojataton kardaast, ʙa ʙuzurgi jod kuned. Va nekukoronro xusxaʙar deh
Xudo az kasone, ki imon ovardaand, difo' mekunad va Xudo xijonatkoroni nosiposro dust nadorad
Ba kasone, ki ʙa cang ʙa sarason toxt ovardaand va mavridi sitam qaror giriftaand, ruxsat doda sud va Xudo ʙar piruz gardonidanason tavonost
Onhoe, ki ʙa nohaq az dijorason ronda sudaand, faqat in ʙud, ki meguftand; «Parvardigori mo Xudoi jaktost?» Va agar Xudo ʙa'zero ʙa vasilai ʙa'ze digar daf' nakarda ʙud, dajrhovu kalisoho va kunisthovu mascidhoe, ki nomi Xudo ʙa farovoni dar on ʙurda mesavad, vajron megardid. Va Xudo har kasro, ki jorias kunad, jori mekunad va Xudo tavonovu piruzmand ast
Hamon kason, ki agar dar zamin qudratason dihem, namoz meguzorand va zakot medihand va amr ʙa ma'rufu nahj az munkar mekunand. Va sarancomi hamai korho ʙo Xudost
Agar inho turo duruƣ ʙarovardaand, pes az onho qavmi Nuh va Od va Samud niz duruƣ ʙarovardaand
va niz qavmi Iʙrohim va qavmi Lut
va mardumi Madjan. Va Muso niz takziʙ gardvd. Man ʙa kofiron muhlat dodam, on goh onhoro furu giriftam. Va uquʙati Man ci guna ʙud
Ci ʙisjor dehahoi zolimro halok kardem va saqfhojason furu rext va ci ʙisjor cohho, ki ʙekora mond va qasrhoi ʙalandi gackorisuda ʙesohiʙ mond
Ojo dar zamin sajr namekunand, to sohiʙi dilhoe gardand, ki ʙa on aql kunand va gushoe, ki ʙo on ʙisnavand? Zero casmho nestand, ki kur mesavand, ʙalki dilhoe, ki dar sinaho coj dorand, kur savand
Az tu ʙa sitoʙ azoʙ metalaʙand va Xudo hargiz va'dai xudro xilof namekunad. Va jak ruz az ruzhoi Parvardigori tu ʙaroʙar ʙo hazor sol ast, az on solhoe, ki mesumured
Ci ʙisjor dehahoe, ki zolim ʙudand va Man muhlatason dodam, on goh onhoro furu giriftam. Va ʙozgasti hama nazdi Man ast
Bigu: «Ej mardum, man ʙaroi sumo ʙimdihandae oskoram»
Pas ononro, ki imon ovardaand va korhoi soista kardaand, ʙaxsoisu rizqe ʙuzurg ast
Va onon, ki dar raddi ojoti Mo mekusand va mexohand Moro ociz kunand, ahli cahannamand
Mo pes az tu har jak rasul jo naʙiero firistodaʙosem, cun ʙa xondani ojot masƣul sud, sajton dar suxani u cize afkand. Va Xudo on ciro, ki sajton afkanda ʙud nasx (rad) kard, sipas ojoti xudro ustovori ʙaxsid va Xudo donovu hakim ast
To ki on ci sajton dar suxani u afkanda, ʙaroi kasone, ki dar qalʙhojason ʙemorist va niz saxtdilon ozmoise ʙosad va sitamkoron dar dusmanie ʙuzurgand
Va to donisjoftagon ʙidonand, ki Qur'on ʙa rosti az coniʙi Parvardigori tust va ʙa on imon ʙijovarand va dilhojason ʙa on orom girad. Va Xudo kasonero, ki imon ovardaand, ʙa rohi rost hidojat mekunad
Hamesa kofiron dar on sak mekunand, to on goh, ki qijomat nogahon ʙar sarason faro rasad jo ʙa azoʙi ruzi ʙesodmoni giriftor ojand
Farmonravoi dar on ruz az oni Xudost. Mijonason hukm mekunad. Pas kasone, ki imon ovardaand va korhoi soista kardaand, dar ʙihisthoi purne'matand
Va kasone, ki kofir sudaand va ojoti Moro duruƣ sumurdaand, ʙarojason azoʙest xorkunanda
Va kasonero, ki dar rohi Xudo muhocirat kardand, sipas kusta sudand jo xud murdand, Xudo ʙa rizqe neku ruzi medihad. Zero Xudo ʙehtarini ruzidihandagon ast
Ononro ʙa coe darovarad, ki az on xusnud ʙosand. Va alʙatta Xudo donovu soʙiraet
Har kas uquʙat kunad, hamcunon ki uro uquʙat kardaand, on goh ʙar u duʙora sitam kunand, Xudo jorias xohad kard. Zero Xudo avfkunanda va omurzanda ast
In ʙa on saʙaʙ ast, ki Xudo az saʙ kam mekunad va ʙa ruz meafzojad va az ruz kam mekunad va ʙa saʙ meafzojad. Va Xudo sunavovu ʙinost
In ʙa on saʙaʙ ast, ki Xudo haq ast va on ci ʙa coi U ʙa xudoi mexonand, ʙotil ast va U ʙalandmartaʙavu ʙuzurg ast
Ojo nadidai, ki Xudo az osmon ʙoron firistod va zamin pursaʙza gardid? Alʙatta Xudo ʙorikʙinu ogoh ast
Az oni Ust on ci dar osmonho va on ci dar zamin ast. Ust ʙenijoz (ʙe ehtijoc) va sazovori sitois
Ojo nadidai, ki Xudo har ciro dar rui zamin ast, romi sumo kardaast va kistihoro, ki dar darjo ʙa farmoni U meravand? Va osmonro nigoh dosta, ki cuz ʙa farmoni U ʙar zamin naaftad. Zero Xudoro ʙar mardum ra'fatu (safqatu) mehruʙonist
Ust on ki sumoro zindagi ʙaxsid va sipas ʙimirond va ʙoz zinda mesozad. Va odami nosukr ast
Baroi har ummate dine nihodem, to ʙar on din ʙosad. Pas dar in kor ʙo tu mucodala nakunand va mardumro ʙa Parvardigori xud da'vat kun, zero tu ʙa rosti ʙar rohi rost qadam menihi
Va agar ʙo tu mucodala kardand, ʙigu: «Xudo ʙar har kore, ki mekuned, ogohtar ast
Dar on ci mavridi ixtilofi sumost, Xudo dar ruzi qijomat hukm xohad kard»
Ojo nadonistai, ki Xudo har ciro, ki dar osmonhovu zamin ast, medonad? Va in dar kitoʙe navistaast va korest ʙar Xudo oson
Va ƣajri Olloh cizero meparastand, ki xec dalele ʙar vucudas nozil nasudaast va hec donise ʙad-on nadorand. Va sitamkoron jovare nadorand
Cun ojoti ravsangari Mo ʙar onon xonda savad, nisoni inkorro ʙar cehrai kofiron mesinosi cunon ki nazdik ʙosad ʙar onon, ki ojotro mexonand, hamlavar savand. Bigu: «Ojo sumoro ʙa cize ʙadtar az in ogoh kunam? Otas. Xudo onro ʙar kasone, ki imon naovardaand, va'da dodaast va otas ʙad sarancomest!»
Ej mardum, misole ova; rda sud. Bad-on gus dihed. Kasone, ki onhoro ʙa coi Olloh ʙa xudoi mexoned, agar hama gird ojand, magasero naxohand ofarid va agar magase cize az onho ʙiraʙojad, ʙozsitondanasro natavonand. Toliʙu matluʙ har du notavonand
Xudoro, cunon ki loiqi Ust, nasinoxtand. Har oina Xudo nerumandu piruz ast
Xudo az mijoni faristagonu mardumon rasulone ixtijor mekunad. Alʙatta Xudo sunavovu ʙinost
On ciro, ki dar pesi rujason ast va on ciro, ki pusti sarason ast, medonad. Va hamai korho ʙad-U ʙozmegardad
Ej kasone, ki imon ovardaed, ruqu' kuned va sacda kuned va Parvardigoratonro ʙiparasted va korhoi nek ʙa coj ovared, ʙosad, ki nacot joʙed
Dar rohi Xudovand, cunon ki ʙojad cihod kuned. U sumoro ʙarguzid. Va ʙarojaton dar din hec tangnoe padid najovard. Dini padaraton Iʙrohim ast. U pes az in va dar in sumoro musalmon nomid. To pajomʙar ʙar sumo guvoh ʙosad va sumo ʙar digar mardum guvoh ʙosed. Pas namoz ʙiguzored va zakot ʙidihed va ʙa Xudo iʙodat kuned! Ust mavloi sumo. Ci mavloe neku va ci jovare neku
Dar haqiqat nacot joftand mu'minon
onon, ki dar namozason tarsu umed mekunand
va onon, ki az ʙehuda ruj megardonand
va onon, ki zakotro medihand
va onon, ki sarmgohi xudro nigoh medorand
ƣajri hamsaron jo kanizoni xud, ki dar nazdiki ʙo onon mavridi malomat qaror namegirand
va kasone, ki ƣajr az in du ʙicujand, az haddi xud tacovuz kardaand
va onon, ki amonatho va pajmonhoi xudro rioja me- kunand
va onon, ki ʙar namozhoi xud davomdihandaand
inho merosʙaron hastand
ki firdavsro, ki hamesa dar on covidonand, ʙa meros meʙarand

sipae uro nutfae dar cojgohe ustuvor qaror do- dem
on goh az on nutfa laxtaxune ofaridem va az on laxtaxun poraguste va az on poragust ustuxonho ofaridem va ustuxonhoro ʙo gust pusonidem; ʙori digar uro ofarinise digar dodem. Sazovori ta'- zim ast Xudovand, on ʙehtarini ofarinandagon
Va ʙa'd az in hamai sumo xohed murd
Boz dar ruzi qijomat zinda megarded
Va ʙar ʙoloi saraton haft osmon ʙijofaridem, hol on ki az in ofarinis ƣofil naʙudaem
Va az osmon ʙa miqdori ehtijoc oʙ firistodem va onro dar zamin coj dodem va Mo ʙar noʙud karda- nas tavono hastem
Bo on oʙ ʙarojaton ʙustonhoe az xurmovu angur pajdo kardem. Sumoro dar on ʙorho mevahoi ʙisjo- rest, ki az onho mexured
Va daraxtest, ki dar Turi Sino merujad. Ravƣan medihad va on ravƣan ʙaroi xurandagon nonxuri- sest
Sumoro dar corpojon iʙratest. Az sire, ki dar sikamason hast, ʙa sumo mepusonem va az onho foida- hoi ʙisjor meʙared va az onho mexured
Va ʙar onho va ʙar kistiho savor mesaved
Qasam, ki Nuhro ʙar qavmas firistodem. Guft: «Ej qavmi man, Xudoi jaktoro ʙiparasted. Sumoro Xudovande ƣajri U nest. Ojo nametarsed?»
Buzurgoni qavmas, ki kofir ʙudand, guftand: «In mard insonest monandi sumo, mexohad az sumo ʙolotar savad. Agar Xudo mexost, farpstago- nero mefiristod. Mo hargiz cunin cize dar ruzgo- ri nijogonamon nasunidaem
U mardi devonae ʙes nest. Jakcand muddat ʙar u saʙr kuned». (to margas faro rasad)
Guft: «Ej Parvardigori man, aknun, ki maro duruƣ meʙarorand, joriam kun»
Ba u vahj kardem, ki kistiro dar huzuri Mo va ʙa ilhomi Mo ʙisoz. Va cun farmoni Mo darra- sid va oʙ az tanur ʙerun zad, az har cinse duto va niz kasoni xudro ʙa on ʙiʙar. Ƣajri on kas, ki pes az in dar ʙorai u suxan raftaast. Va dar ʙorai si- tamkoron ʙo Man suxan maguj, ki onho hama ƣarq- sudagonand
Cun xud va hamrohonat ʙa kisti nisasted, ʙi- gu: «Sukr Xudojro, ki moro az mardumi zolim nacot ʙaxsid»
Va ʙigu: «Ej Parvardigori man, maro furud ovar dar cojgohe muʙorak, ki tu ʙehtarini faroran- dagoni»
Dar in doston iʙrathovu pandhost va mo tanho ozmojandagone ʙudem
Va ʙa'd az onho mardume digar ʙijofaridem
Va az xudason ʙa mijonason pajomʙare firisto- dem, ki Xudoi jaktoro ʙiparasted, sumoro xudoe cuz U nest. Ojo nametarsed
Guruhe az ʙuzurgoni qavmas, ki kofir ʙudand va didori oxiratro duruƣ mesumurdand va dar in dunjojason ajsu ne'mat doda ʙudem, guftand: «In mard insonest monandi sumo, az on ci mexured, mexurad va az on ci meosomed. meosomad
Va agar ʙa insone monandi xud ito'at kuned, zijon kardaed
Ojo ʙa sumo va'da medihad, ki cun murded va xoku ustuxon suded, sumoro az gur ʙerun meova- rand
In va'dae, ki ʙa sumo doda suda, dur ast, dur
Cuz hamin zindagonii dunjavii mo hec nest, ʙa dunjo meoemu memirem va digar ʙor zinda namesa- vem
In mardest, ki ʙa xudoi jakto duruƣ meʙofad va mo ʙa u imon nameovarem»
Guft: «Ej Parvardigori man, aknun ki maro du- ruƣ meʙarorand, joriam kun!»
Guft: «Ba hamin zudi az karda pusajmon mesa- vand»
Pas ʙa haq sadoe saxt ononro furu girift. Mo- nandi gijoh xuskason kardem. Ej, nasiʙi mardumi sitamkora duri az rahmati Xudo ʙod
Va ʙa'd az onho mardume digar ʙijofaridem
Hec millate az acali xud na pes meaftad va na dertar mekunad
Sipas paj dar paj pajomʙaroni xudro firisto- dem. Har ʙor, ki pajomʙare ʙar millate omad, duruƣ ʙarovardand va Mo niz onhoro az pasi jakdigar ʙa halokat rasonidem va ononro dostonho kardem. Ej, nasiʙi mardume, ki imon nameovaravdd, duri az rahmati Xudo ʙod
On goh Muso va ʙarodaras Horunro ʙo ojoti Xud va dalelhoi ravsan firistodem
nazdi Fir'avn va ʙuzurgoni qavmas. Pas gar- dankasi kardaid, kn mardume ʙartaricuj ʙudand
va guftand: «Ojo ʙa du inson, ki monandi mo hastand va qavmason ʙandagoni mo ʙudand, imon ʙijovarem?»
Onhoro duruƣ ʙarovardand va xudro ʙa halokat afkandand
Alʙatta Mo ʙa Muso kitoʙ dodem, ʙosad, ki hi- dojat joʙand
Va pisari Marjam va modarasro mu'cizae soxtem va on duro ʙar ʙaland coe, ki qarorgohe va oʙi ravon dost coj dodem
Ej pajomʙaron, az cizhoi pokizavu xus ʙixured va korhoi soista kuned, ki Man ʙa korhoe, ki me- kuned, ogoham
Alʙatta in dini sumo dinest jagona va Man Parvardigori sumojam, az Man ʙitarsed
Pas dini xudro firqa-firqa kardand va har firqae ʙa ravise, ki intixoʙ karda ʙud, dilxus ʙud
Ononro to cande dar gumrohijason ʙiguzor
Ojo mepindorand, ki on molu farzand, ki ʙa onho dodem
ʙaroi on ast, ki mekusem xajre ʙa onho ʙiraso- nem? Na, onon darnamejoʙand
Onhoe, ki az xavfi Parvardigorason larzonand
va onhoe, ki ʙa ojoti Parvardigorason imon me- ovarand
va onhoe, ki ʙa Parvardigorason sirk nameova- rand
va onhoe, ki hamai on ciro ʙojad ado kunand, ado mekunand va ʙoz ham dilhojason tarson ast, ki ʙojad nazdi Parvardigorason ʙozgardand
inho hastand, ki ʙa korhoi nek mesitoʙand va dar on ʙar jakdigar pesi mecujand
Bar hec kas cuz ʙa miqdori tavonas taklif na- mekunem. Va nazdi Mo kitoʙest, ki ʙa haq suxan megujad. Va ʙar onho sitame nameravad
Na! Dilhojason az in suxan dar pardai ƣaflat ast. Va onhoro korhoest cuz in korho, ki mekunand
To on goh ki sarvatmandonasonro ʙa azoʙ gi- riftor kunem va nola sar dihand
Imruz nola sar madihed, ki sumoro az azoʙi Mo kas nacot nadihad
Ojoti Man! ʙarojatjun xonda, mesud va sumo name- pazirufted va pas-pas merafted
Bar on takaʙʙur mekarded va saʙhangom dar af- sonasaroi nosazo megufted
Ojo dar in suxan nameandesand jo ʙaroi onho ci- ze nozil suda, ki ʙaroi nijogonason nozil nasuda ʙud
Jo on ki pajomʙarasonro nasinoxtaand, ki inko- ras mekunand
Jo megujand, ki devona ast? Na, pajomʙarason ʙa dini haq ʙar onho firistoda sud, vale ʙestara- son az haq ʙadʙini dorand
Agar haq az pai havashojason meraft, osmonho- vu zamin va har ki dar onhost, halok mesud. Vale Mo pan; das, on firistodem va onho az pandason rujgardon sudand
Jo tu az onho muzde metalaʙi? Muzdi Parvardi- gorat ʙehtar ast, ki U ʙehtarini ruzidihandagon ast
Alʙatta tu ʙa rohi rostason da'vat mekuni
Va kasone, ki ʙa oxirat imon nadorand, az rohi rost kacravand
Agar ʙar onho rahmat meovarem va ozorero, ki ʙa on giriftorand, az onho dur mesoxtem, ʙoz ham xamcunon ʙo sarsaxti dar tacovuzi xud sargasta me- mondand
Ba azoʙ giriftorason kardem na sar xam kar- dand va na iltico
To on goh ki dare az azoʙi saxt ʙa rujason ku- sodem, cunon ki az hama co noumed gastand
Va ust on Xudoe, ki ʙarojaton gusu casmu dil ʙijofarid. Ci andak sukr meguzored
Ust on Xudoe, ki sumoro dar rui zamin xalq kard va hama nazdi U cam' ovarda mesaved
Va Ust on Xudoe, ki zinda mekunad va memiro- nad va omadusudi saʙu ruz az Ust, Caro aql namekuned
Na, onho niz hamon suxanon guftand, ki pesi- nijon meguftand
Guftand: «Ojo agar mo ʙimirem va xoku ustuxon savem, ʙoz ham zinda mesavem?»
Ba mo va padaronamon niz pes az in cunin va'- dahoe doda suda ʙud. Inho cize cuz afsonahoi pe- sinijon nest!»
Bigu: «-Agar medoned, in zamin va har ki dar on ast, az oni kist?»
Xohand guft: «Az oni Xudo». Bigu: «Ojo pand na- megired?»
Bigu: «Kist Parvardigori haft osmon va Par- vardigori arsi ʙuzurg?»
Xohand guft: «Xudo». Bigu: «Ojo nametarsed?»
Bigu: «Agar medoned, podsohii hama cizho ʙa dasti kist? Kist on, ki ʙa hama kas panoh dihad va kasero az u panoh nest?»
Xohand guft: «Xudo». Bigu: «Pas caro fireʙ me- xured?»
Na! Mo ʙar onho suxani rost firistodem va onho duruƣ megujand
Xudo hec farzande nadorad va hec xudoe ʙo U nest. Agar cunin meʙud har xudoe ʙo ofaridagoni xud ʙa jak su mekasid va ʙar jakdigar ʙolotarsaviro mecustand. Xudo az on guna, ki Uro vasf mekunand, pok ast
Donoi pinhonu oskoro, az har ci sariki U me- sozand, ʙolotar ast
Bigu: «Ej Parvardigori, man, kos cizero, ki ʙa onon va'da doda suda, ʙa man nison medodi
Pas, ej Parvardigori man, maro dar zumrai si- tamkoron qaror madeh»
Va Mo agar ʙixohem, ki on ciro ʙa onon va'da dodaem, turo nison dihem, metavonem
Suxani ʙadi onhoro ʙar har ci nekutar meojad, cavoʙ deh. Mo ʙa suxani onho ogohtar hastem
Bigu: «Ej Parvardigori man, az vasvasahoi saj- ton ʙa tu panoh meovaram
Va ʙa Tu panoh meovaram, ej Parvardigori man, agar nazdi man hozir ojand!»
Cun jakeasonro marg faro rasad, gujad: «Ej Par- vardigori man, maro ʙozgardon. (ʙa hajot)
Sojad korhoi soistaero, ki tark karda ʙudam, ʙa coj ovaram». Hargiz! In suxanest, ki u megujad va pusti sarason to ruzi qijomat mone'est, ki ʙozgast natavonand
Cun dar sur damida savad, hec xesovande mijo- nason namonad va hec az xoli jakdigar napursand
Onon, ki tarozujason sangin ʙosad, xud nacotjof- tagonand
Va onon, ki tarozujason saʙuk ʙosad, ʙa xud zijon rasokidaand va dar cahannam covid monda- gonand
Otas cehrahojasonro mesuzonad va dar duzax tursrujand
Ojo ojathoi Man ʙarojaton xonda namesud va onho- ro duruƣ mehisoʙided
Gujand: «Ej Parvardigori mo, surʙaxtijamon ʙar mo ƣalaʙa kard va mo mardume gumroh ʙudem
Ej Parvardigori mo, moro az in otas ʙerun ovar. Agar digar ʙor cunon kardem, az zolimon ʙosem»
Gujad: «Dar otas gum saved va ʙo Man suxan nagued»
Ore, guruhe az ʙandagoni Man meguftand: «Ej Parvardigori mo, imon ovardem, moro ʙiʙaxso va ʙar mo rahmat ovar, ki Tu ʙehtarini rahmovaran- dagoni»
Va sumo masxaraason mekarded to jodi Maro az xotiraton raʙudand. Va sumo hamcunon ʙa onho mexandided
Imruz onhoro ʙa xotiri saʙre, ki mekardand, muzd mediham. Onho ʙa murodi xud rasidaand
Gujad: «Ba sumori solho ci muddat dar zamin zistaed?»
Gujand: «Jak ruz jo qijomate az jak ruz. Az onho, ki mesumurdand, ʙipurs»
Gujad: «Agar ogohi dosted, medonisted, ki cuz andake nazistaed
Ojo pin d ore d, ki sumoro ʙehuda ofaridaem va sumo ʙa nazdi Mo ʙozgardonida namesaved?»
Pas pok ast Xudoi jakto — on farmonravoi rostin. Hec xudoe cuz U nest! Parvardigori arsi ʙuzurgvor ast
On kas, ki ʙa coi Xudoi jakto xudoi digarero me- xonad, va ʙa haqqonijatas hec ʙurhone nadorad, in ast, ki hisoʙas nazdi Parvardigoras xo- had ʙud. Va kofiron nacot namejoʙand
Va ʙigu: «Ej Parvardigori man, ʙiʙaxsovu rah- mat kun va Tu ʙehtarini rahmatkunandagon has- ti!»
Suraest, ki onro nozil kardaem va vociʙas soxtaem va dar on ojote ravsan firistodaem, ʙosad, ki pand gired
Zanu mardi zinokorro har jakro sad zarʙa ʙizaned. Va agar ʙa Xudovu ruzi qijomat imon dored, maʙod, ki dar hukmi Xudo nisʙat ʙa on du rahmdil garded. Va ʙojad, ki ʙa hangomi sikanca kardanason guruhe az mu'minon hozir ʙosand
Mardi zinokor ƣajri zani zinokor jo musrikro namegirad va zani zinokorro ƣajri mardi zinokor jo musrik namegirad. Va in ʙar mu'minon harom sudast
Kasonero, ki zanoni pokro ʙa zino mutahham mekunand va cahor sohid nameovarand, hastod zarʙa ʙizaned va az on pas hargiz sohidiasonro napazired, ki mardume fosiqand
Ƣajri kasone, ki ʙa'd, az on tavʙa kunand va ʙa isloh ojand. Zero Xudo ʙaxsojandavu mehruʙon ast
Va kasone, ki zanoni xudro ʙa zino mutahham mekunand va sohide cuz xud nadorand, har jak az onhoro cahor ʙor sohidi ast ʙa nomi Xudo, ki az rostgujon ast
Va ʙori pancum ʙigujad, ki la'nati Xudo ʙar u ʙod, agar az duruƣgujon ʙosad
Va agar on zan cahor ʙor ʙa Xudo savgand xurad, ki on mard duruƣ megujad, cazo az u ʙardosta mesavad
Va ʙori pancum ʙigujad, ki xasmi Xudo ʙar u ʙod, agar mard az rostgujon ʙosad
Halok mesuded agar fazlu rahmate, ki Xudo ʙar sumo dodaast, nameʙud? Va agar Xudo tavʙapaziru hakim nameʙud
Kasone, ki on duruƣi ʙuzurgro soxtaand, guruhe az sumojand. Mapindored, ki sumoro dar on sarre ʙuvad. Na, xajri sumo dar on ʙuvad. Har marde az onho ʙa on andoza gunoh, ki kardaast, ʙa cazo rasad va az mijoni onho, on ki ʙestarini in ʙuhtonro ʙa uhda dorad ʙa azoʙe ʙuzurg giriftor meojad
Caro hangome ki on ʙuhtonro sunided, mardonu zanoni mu'min ʙa xud gumoni nek naʙurdand va naguftand, ki in tuhmate oskor ast
Caro cahor sohid ʙar idda'oi xud najovardand? Pas agar sohidone najovardaand, dar nazdi Xudo dar zumrai duruƣgujonand
Agar fazlu rahmati Xudo dar dunjovu oxirat nameʙud, ʙa sazoi on suxanon, ki megufted, sumoro azoʙe ʙuzurg darmerasid
On goh, ki on suxanro az dahoni jakdigar megirifted va cize ʙar zaʙon meronded, ki dar ʙorai on hec, namedonisted va mepindosted, ki kore xurd ast va hol on, ki dar nazdi Xudo kore ʙuzurg ʙud
Caro on goh ki suxan sunided, nagufted: «Moro nasojad, ki onro ʙozguem, Parvardigoro, Tu poki, in tuhmate ʙuzurg ast?»
Xudo sumoro pand medihad, ki agar az muʹminon hasted, ʙori digar girdi cunon kore magarded
Xudo ojotro ʙaron sumo ʙajon mekunad va Xudo donovu hakim ast
Baroi kasone, ki dust dorand, dar ʙorai mu'minon tuhmati zino pahn savad, dar dunjovu oxirat azoʙe dardovar muhajjost. Xudo medonad, va sumo namedoned
Halok mesuded, agar fazlu rahmate, ki Xudo ʙa sumo dodaast, nameʙud. Va agar Xudo mehruʙonu ʙaxsojanda nameʙud
Ej kasone, ki imon ovardaed, poj ʙa coi poi sajton maguzored. Va har ki poj ʙa coi poi sajton guzorad, ʙidonad, ki u ʙa fahsovu munkar (korhoi ʙad) farmon medihad. Va agar fazlu rahmate ki Xudo ʙar sumo arzoni dostaast, nameʙud, hec jak az sumo hargiz rui poki namedid. Vale Xudo har kasro, ki ʙixohad, pokiza mesozad. Va Xudo sunavovu donost
Tavongaron va onon, ki kusoise dar kori onhost, naʙojad savgand ʙixurand, ki ʙa xesovandonu miskinon va muhociron dar rohi Xudo cize nadihand. Bojad ʙiʙaxsandu ʙiʙaxsojand. Ojo namexohed, ki Xudo sumoro ʙiʙaxsojad? Va Xudost ʙaxsojandai mehruʙon
Kasone, ki ʙar zanoni pokdoman va ʙexaʙar az zino va mu'min tuhmati zino mezanand, dar dunjovu oxirat la'nat sudaand va ʙarojason azoʙest ʙuzurg
ruze, ki zaʙonason va dasthojasonu pojhojason ʙar ziddason ʙar korhoe, ki mekardaand, sohidi dihand
On ruz, ki Xudo cazojasonro ʙa tamomi ʙidihad va ʙidonand, ki Xudo haqiqati oskor ast
Zanoni nopok ʙaroi mardoni nopok va mardoni nopok ʙaroi zanoni nopok va zanoni pok ʙaroi mardoni pok va mardoni pok ʙaroi zanoni pok. Onho az on ci dar ʙoraason megujand, pokand. Baxsoisu rizqi neku ʙaroi onhost
Ej kasone, ki imon ovardaed, ʙa xonae ƣajr az xonai xud ʙe on, ki icozat talaʙida va ʙar sokinonas salom karda ʙosed, nadaroed. In ʙaroi sumo ʙehtar ast, ʙosad, ki pand gired
Va agar dar xona kasero najofted, doxil nasaved to sumoro ruxsat dihand. Va agar gujand: «Bozgarded», ʙozgarded, in ʙarojaton pokizatar ast. Va Xudo ʙa har kore, ki mekuned, ogoh ast
Bar sumo gunohe nest, agar ʙa xonahoi ƣajrimaskun, ki mato'e dar on dored, doxil saved. Har ciro oskor sozed, jo pinhon dored. Xudo ʙa on ogoh ast
Ba mardoni mu'min ʙigu, ki casmoni xud ʙipusand va sarmgohi xud iigah dorand. In ʙarojason pokizatar ast. Zero Xudo ʙa korhoe, ki mekunand, ogoh ast
Va ʙa zanoni mu'min ʙigu, ki casmoni xud ʙipusand va sarmgohi xud nigoh dorand va zinathoi xudro cuz on miqdor, ki pajdost, oskor nakunand va miqna'ahoi (rujmolhoi) xudro to gireʙon ʙipusand va zinathoi xudro oskor nakunand, ƣajri ʙa savhari xud jo padari xud jo padari savhari xud jo pisari xud jo pisari savhari xud jo ʙarodari xud jo pisari ʙarodari xud jo pisari xohari xud jo zanoni hamdini xud, jo ʙandagoni xud jo mardoni xidmatguzori xud, ki raƣʙat ʙa zan nadorand, jo kudakone, ki az sarmgohi zanon ʙexaʙarand. Va niz cunon poj ʙar zamin nazanand to on zinat, ki piihon kardaand, donista savad. Ej mu'minon, hamagon ʙa dargohi Xudo tavʙa kuned, sojad nacot joʙed
Bezanonatonro va ƣulomu kanizoni xudro, ki soista ʙosand, hamsar dihed. Agar ʙenavo ʙosand, Xudo ʙa karami xud tavongarason xohad soxt, ki Xudo kusoisdihanda va donost
Onon, ki tavonoii zanosui nadorand, ʙojad pokDomani pesa kunand, to Xudo az karami xud tavongarason gardonad. Va az ʙandagonaton onon, ki xohoni ʙozxaridani xudand, agar dar onho xajre jofted, ʙozxaridanasonro ʙipazired. Va az on mol, ki Xudo ʙa sumo arzoni dostaast, ʙa onon ʙidihed. Va kanizoni xudro agar xohand, ki parhezgor ʙosand, ʙa xotiri sarvati dunjavi ʙa zino macʙur nakuned. Har kas, ki ononro ʙa zino vodorad, Xudo ʙaroi on kanizon, ki ʙa macʙuri ʙa on kor vodor gastaand, ʙaxsojandavu mehruʙon ast
Ba tahqiq ʙaroi sumo ojote ravsan va dostonhoe az kasone, ki pes az sumo ʙudaand, va niz pandhoe ʙaroi parhezgoron nozil kardem
Xudo nuri osmonhovu zamin ast. Misoli nuri U cun caroƣdonest, ki dar on caroƣe ʙosad, on caroƣ daruni sisae va on sisa cun sitorae duraxsanda. Az ravƣani daraxti purʙarakati zajtun, ki na sarqi astu na ƣarʙi afruxta ʙosad. Ravƣanas ravsani ʙaxsad, harcand otas ʙa on narasida ʙosad. Nur ʙar ʙoloi nur. Xudo har kasro, ki ʙixohad, ʙa on nur roh menamojad va ʙaroi mardum misolho meovarad. Zero ʙa har cize ogoh ast
On nur dar xonahoest, ki Xudo ruxsat dod ʙaland ʙardorand va nomas dar on co jod savad va Uro har ʙomdodu saʙongoh tasʙeh gujand
Mardone, ki hec ticorat va xaridu furuxte az jodi Xudo va namoz guzoridanu zakot dodaj ʙozason nadorad, az ruze, ki dilhovu didagon digargun mesavand, metarsand
To Xudo ʙa nekutar az on ci kardaand, cazojason dihad va az fazli xud ʙar on ʙiafzojad va Xudo har kiro xohad, ʙehisoʙ ruzi dihad
Amalhoi kofiron cun saroʙest (mavci ƣarmi) dar ʙijoʙone. Tasna oʙas pindorad va cun ʙa on nazdik savad, hec najoʙad va Xudoro nazdi xud joʙad, pas cazoi uro ʙa tamom ʙidihad. Va Xudo zud ʙa hisoʙho merasad
Jo monandi torikihoest dar darjoe cuqur, ki mavcas pusonad va ʙar ʙoloi on mavce digar va ʙar ʙolojas aʙrest tira, torikihoe ʙar ʙoloi jakdigar, on tavr, ki agar dasti xud ʙe? run orad onro natavonad did. Va on, ki Xudo rohasro ʙa hec nure ravsan nakarda ʙosad, hec nure ʙar rohi xud najoʙad
Ojo nadidai, ki har ci dar osmonhovu zamin ast va niz murƣone, ki dar parvozand, tasʙehgui Xudo hastand? Hama namozu tasʙehi Uro medonand. Va Xudo ʙa har kore, ki mokunand, oƣoh ast
Az oni Xudost farmonravoii osmonhovu zamin va ʙozgasti hamagon nazdi Ust
Ojo nadidai, ki Xudo aʙrhoero ʙa ohistagi meronad, on goh, onhoro ʙa ham mepajvandad va aʙre ʙuzurg padid meovarad va ʙoronro ʙini, ki dar on cost, tagarg (ƶola) mefiristad va har kiro xohad, ʙo on mezanad va az har ki mexohad, ʙozas medorad. Rusnoii ʙarqas nazdik ʙosad, ki didagonro kur sozad
Xudo saʙu ruzro megardonad. Xiradmandonro dar in iʙratest
Va Xudo har cunʙandaero az oʙ ʙijofarid Ba'ze az onho ʙar sikam meravand va ʙa'ze ʙar du po meravand va ʙa'ze ʙar cahor po meravand. Xudo har ci ʙixohad, meofarinad. Zero Xudo ʙar har kore tavonost
Ba tazdik ojote ravsangar nozil kardem va Xudo har kasro, ki ʙixohad, ʙa rohi rost hidojat mekunad
Va megujand: «Ba Xudovu pajomʙaras imon ovardaem va ito'at mekunem». Pae az on guruhe az onho ʙozmegardand. Va inho imon najovardaand
Cun onhoro ʙa Xudovu pajomʙaras da'vat kunand, to mijonason hukm kunad, ʙini, ki guruhe rujgardoni mekunand
Va agar haq ʙo onho ʙosad, meojand va ʙa hukm gardan menihand
Ojo dar dilhojason marazest jo dar sak hastand jo ʙimi on dorand, ki Xudovu pajomʙaras ʙar onho zulm kunand? Na, onon xud zolimonand
Cun mu'minonro ʙa Xudovu pajomʙaras da'vat kunand, to mijonason hukm kunad, suxanason ƣajri in nest, ki megujand: «Sunidem va ito'at kardem», inho nacotjoftagonand
Va kasone, ki ʙa Xudovu pajomʙaras farmonʙardorand va az Xudo metarsand va parhezgori mekunand, nacotjoftagonand
Ba Xudo qasam xurdand, qasamhoi saxt, ki agar ʙa onho farmon dihi, az dijori xud ʙerun ravand. Bigu: «Qasam naxured, to'ate sazovor ʙa co ored. Xudo ʙa korhoe, ki mekuned, ogoh ast!»
Bigu: «Ba Xudo ito'at kuned va ʙa pajomʙar ito'at kuned. Pas agar rujgardon saved, ʙar pajomʙar ast on ci ʙa u taklif kardaand va ʙar sumost on ci ʙar sumo taklif kardaand. Va agar ʙa u ito'at kuned, hidojat joʙed. Va ʙar uhdai pajomʙar ƣajri taʙliƣi oskor hec nest»
Xudo ʙa kasone az sumo, ki imon ovardaand va korhoe soista kardaand, va'da dod, ki dar rui zamin conisini digaronason kunad, hamcunon, ki mardumero, ki pes az onho ʙudand, conisini digaron kard, Va dinasonro, ki xud ʙarojason pisandida ast, ustuvor sozad. Va vahsatasonro ʙa tinci ivaz kunad. Maro meparastand va hec cizero ʙo Man sarik namekunand. Va onho, ki az in pas nosukri kunand, nofarmonand
Va namoz ʙiguzored ra zakot ʙidihed va ʙa pajomʙar ito'at kuned, ʙosad, ki ʙar sumo rahmat ovarand
Mapindor, ki kofiron metavonand dar in sarzamin ʙa coe ʙigurezand. Cojgohason cahannam ast va ci ʙad sarancomest
Ej kasone, ki imon ovardaed, ʙojad ƣulomoni sumo va onho, ki hanuz ʙa haddi ʙuluƣ narasidaand, dar se hangom az sumo ʙaroi doxil sudan ʙa xona ruxsat talaʙand: pes az namozi suʙh va hangomi zuhr, ki liʙos az tan ʙerun mekuned va ʙa'd az namozi xuftan. In se vaqt vaqti xilvati sumost. Dar ƣajri on se hangom sumo va onho gunohe nakardaed, agar ʙar jakdigar ʙigzared. Xudo ojotro incunin ʙaroi sumo ʙajon mekunad. Va Xudo donovu hakim ast
Va cun atfoli sumo ʙa haddi ʙuluƣ rasidand, ʙojad monandi kasone, ki zikrason guzast, ruxsat talaʙand. Xudo ojotro incunin ʙaroi sumo ʙajon mekunad. Va Xudo donovu hakim ast
Pirazanon, ki digar umedi suj kardanason nest, ʙe on, ki zinathoi xudro oskor kunand, agar codari xud ʙinihand, gunohe nakardaand. Va xuddori kardan ʙarojason ʙehtar ast va Xudo sunavovu donost
Bar noʙino harace (gunohe) nest va ʙar lang gunohe nest va ʙar ʙemor gunohe nest. Va ʙar sumo gunohe nest, agar az xonai xud jo xonai padaraton jo xonai modaraton jo xonai ʙarodaraton jo xonai xoharaton jo xonai amakaton jo xonai ammaaton jo xonai doijaton (taƣojaton) jo xonai xolaaton jo xonae, ki kalidhoi on nazdi sumost, jo xonai dustaton cize ʙixured. Va gunohe ʙar sumo nest, agar ʙo ham ʙixured jo cudo-cudo. Va cun ʙa xonae doxil saved, ʙar jakdigar salom kuned. in salomest muʙorak va pokiza az coniʙi Xudo. Xudo ojotro ʙaroi sumo incunin ʙajon mekunad, sojad, ki aql kuned
Mu'minon kasone hastand, ki ʙa Xudovu pajomʙaras imon ovardaand va cun ʙo pajomʙar dar kore jakcoja ʙosand, to az u ruxsat natalaʙidaand, naʙojad ʙiravand. Onho, ki az tu ruxsat metalaʙand, kasone hastand, ki ʙa Xudovu pajomʙaras imon ovardaand. Pas hangome ki az tu ʙaroi ʙa'ze az korhojason ruxsat xostand, ʙar har jak az onon, ki xohi, ruxsat ʙideh va ʙarojason az Xudo ʙaxsois ʙixoh ki Xudo ʙaxsojandavu mehruʙon ast
Oncunon ki jakdigarro sado mekuned, pajomʙarro sado nakuned. Xudo medonad ci kasone az sumo dar panohi digare xudro pinhon mesozand va ohistaohista ʙerun meravand. Onon, ki az farmoni U sarpeci mekunand, ʙojad ʙitarsand, ki maʙodo ʙa onho fitnae jo azoʙe dardovar ʙirasad
Az oni Xudost har ci dar osmonhovu zamin ast. Medonad, ki sumo ʙar ci kored. Va on ruz, ki ʙa U ʙozgardonda savand, ononro az korhoe, ki kardaand, ogoh sozad. Va Xudo ʙar har cize donost
Buzurg astu ʙuzurgvor on kas, ki in furqonro ʙar ʙandai Xud nozil kard, to cahonijonro ʙimdihandae ʙosad
On kas, ki az oni Ust farmonravoii osmonhovu zamin va farzande nagiriftaast va Uro sarike dar farmonravoi nest va har cizro ʙijofaridaast va onro ʙa miqdor ofaridaast
Ƣajri U xudojone digar giriftand, ki hec ciz nameofarinand, va xud maxluqand. Na moliki zijoni xud hastand va na naf'i xud va moliki margu zindagi va qijomat nestand
Va kofiron guftand, ki in cuz duruƣe, ki xud ʙoftaast va guruhe digar uro ʙar on jori dodaand, hec nest. Haqqo, on ci megujand, sitamu ʙotil ast
Ba guftand: «In afsonahoi pesinijon ast, ki har suʙhu som ʙar u xonda mesavad va u menavisadas»
Bigu: «In kitoʙro kase nozil kardaast, ki nihoni osmonhovu zaminro medonad va ʙaxsojandavu mehruʙon ast!»
Guftand: «Caro in pajomʙar, ƣizo mexurad va dar ʙozorho roh meravad? Caro faristae ʙar u furud nameojad to ʙo u ʙimdihanda ʙosad
Caro az osmon gance ʙarojas afkanda nasavad? Caro uro ʙoƣe nest, ki az on ʙixurad?» Va sitamkoron guftand: «Sumo ʙa mardi codusudae pajravi mekuned!»
Bingar, ki ci guna ʙarojat dostonho meovarand. Gumroh sudaand va tavoni roh joftanason nest
Buzurgu ʙuzurgvor ast on kas, ki agar xohad, ʙehtar az on ʙa tu medihad — ʙoƣhoe, ki dar onho nahrho cori ʙosad va ʙarojat qasrho ʙiofarinad
Balki inho qijomatro duruƣ hisoʙand. Va Mo ʙaroi kanone, ki qijomatro duruƣ hisoʙand, otasi suzon omoda kardaem
ki cun az rohi dur ʙuʙinadason, cusisu xurusasro ʙisnavand
Va cun dastho ʙar gardan ʙasta dar tangie az on aftand, ʙa du'o margi xud mexohand
Imruz na jak ʙor margi xud xohed, margi xud farovon xohed
Bigu: «Ojo in ʙehtar ast jo on ʙihisti covidon, ki ʙa parhezgoron va'da sudaast, ki mukofotu sarancomi onon xohad ʙud?»
To aʙad har ci ʙixohand, dar on co hast. Va'daest, ki ancom dodani on az Parvardigorat xosta sudaast
Ruze, ki ononro ʙo cizhoe, ki ƣajri Xudoi jakto meparastidand, ʙa mashar cam' ovard va sipas pursad: «Ojo sumo in ʙandagoni Maro gumroh mekarded, jo onho xud rohro gum karda ʙudand?»
Gujand: «Poki Tu! Moro sazovor naʙudaast, ki cuz tu kasero ʙa jori girem. Tu xud onho va padaronasonro ʙarxurdor soxti, cunon ki jodi Turo faromus kardand va mardume sudand ʙa halokat aftoda
Inho on ciro megufted, duruƣ xondand va aknun natavoned azoʙero az xud dur sozed jo xudro jori dihed. Va har kas az sumo, ki sitam kunad, azoʙe ʙuzurgas mecasonem
Pes az tu pajomʙarone firistodaem, ki ta'om mexurdand va dar ʙozorho roh meraftand. Va sumoro vasilai ozmoisi jakdigar qaror dodem. Ojo saʙr tavoned kard? Va Parvardigori tu ʙinost
Kasone, ki ʙa didori Mo umed nadorand, guftand: «Caro faristagon ʙar mo namefarojand? Jo caro Parvardigori xudro nameʙinem?» Ba rosti, ki xudro ʙuzurg sumurdand va sarkasi kardand, sarkasie ʙuzurg
Ruze, ki faristagonro ʙuʙinand, dar on ruz gunahkoronro hec xusxaʙare nadihand va ʙa inho gujand: «Xusxaʙar ʙar sumo harom ast!»
Z Va ʙa a'mole, ki kardaand, qasd kunem va hamaro cun zarroti xok ʙarʙod dihem
Ahli ʙihist dar in ruz dar ʙehtarin cojgoh va ʙehtarin makon ʙaroi oromis hastand
Ruze, ki osmon ʙo aʙrho mesikofad va faristagon ʙar zamin pojon firistoda savand
farmonravoi dar on ruz, ʙa rosti, az oni Xudoi rahmon ast. Va ʙaroi kofiron ruze dusvor xohad ʙud
Ruze, ki kofir dastoni xudro ʙa dandon gazad va gujad: «Ej kos, rohero, ki rasul dar pes girifta ʙud dar roh girifta ʙudam
Voj ʙar man, kos falonro dust namegiriftam
ʙo on ki Qur'on ʙaroi man nozil suda ʙud, maro az pajravias ʙozmedost. Va in sajton hamesa odamiro xoru tanho meguzorad
Pajomʙar guft: «Ej Parvardigori man qavmi man tarki Qur'on guftand!»
Incunin har pajomʙarero az mijoni kofiron dusmane padid ovardem. Va Parvardigori tu ʙaroi rohnamoivu jorii tu kofist
Kofiron guftand: «Caro in Qur'on ʙa jakʙora ʙar u nozil namesavad?» Baroi on ast, ki dili turo ʙa on ustuvori dihem va onro ʙa ohistagivu tartiʙ xonem
Har misole ʙaroi tu ʙijovarand, alʙatta cavoʙasro ʙa rosti va nekutarin ʙajon ʙijovarem
Kasonero, ki az ruj mekasandu dar cahannam cam' meovarand, ʙa cojgoh ʙadtaru ʙa roh gumgastatarand
Ba Muso kitoʙ dodem va ʙarodaras Horunro madadgoras soxtem
Va guftem: «Nazdi mardume, ki ojoti Moro duruƣ ʙarovardaand, ʙiraved». Va on qavmro ʙa saxti halok kardem
Qavmi Nuhro, cun pajomʙaronro duruƣ ʙarovardand, ƣark kardem va onhoro ʙaroi mardum iʙrate soxtem. Va ʙaroi sitamkoron azoʙe dardovar omoda kardaem
va Odro va Samudro va ashoʙi Rassro va naslhoi ʙisjorero, ki mijoni onho ʙudand, halok kardem
Va ʙaroi hama misolhoe ovardem va hamaro nestu noʙud soxtem
Va ʙar dehae, ki ʙar on ʙoroni azoʙ ʙorida ʙudem, guzar mekardand. Ojo onro namedidand? Ore, ʙa qijomat umed nadostand
Cun turo didand, masxaraat kardand, ki ojo in ast on pajomʙare, ki Xudo ʙar mo firistoda ast
Agar ʙar xudojonamon ustuvor nameistodem, nazdiq ʙud, ki moro az parastisason gumroh kunad. Cun azoʙro ʙuʙinand, xohand donist ci kase gumrohtar ʙudaast
Ojo on kasro, ki havoi nafsro ʙa xudoi girifta ʙud, didi? Ojo tu zomini u hasti
Jo gumon kardai, ki ʙestarinason mesunavandu mefahmand? Inho cun corpojone hastand, ʙalki az corpojon ham gumrohtarand
Nadidai, ki Parvardigori tu ci guna sojaro mekasad? Agar mexost, dar jak co sokinas megardond. On goh oftoʙro ʙar u dalel gardonidem
Sipas ʙargirkftemas, giriftane andak-andak
Ust, ki saʙro pusisi sumo kard va xoʙro oromisaton va ruzro zamoni ʙarxostanaton
Ust, ki pesopesi rahmati xud ʙodhoro ʙa muƶda dodan firistod. Va az osmon oʙe pok nozil kardem
to sarzamini murdaro ʙa on hajot ʙaxsem va corpojon va mardumi ʙisjorero, ki ofaridaem, az on oʙ dihem
Va to ʙa tafakkur pardozand, ʙoronro mijonason taqsim kardem. Vale ʙestari mardum nosiposi kardand
Agar mexostem, ʙa har dehae ʙimdihandae mefiristodem
Ba kofiron ito'at makun va ʙa hukmi Xudo ʙo onho cihod kun, cihode ʙuzurg
Ust, ki du darjo ʙa ham ʙijomext — jake sirinu guvoro va digare suroʙe saxt gazanda. Va mijoni on du mrne'ae va sadde ustuvor qaror dod
Ust, ki odamiro az oʙ ʙijofarid va uro nasaʙu pajvand soxt va Parvardigori tu ʙa in korho tavonost
Ƣajri Xudoi jakto cizhoero meparastand, ki ʙa onho na naf' medihad va na zijon. Va kofir hamesa jorirasoni muxolifoni Parvardigori xud. ast
Mo turo firistodem, ʙaroi on ki xusxaʙar dihi va ʙitarsoni
Bigu: «Man az sumo hec muzde nametalaʙam lekin harki xohad, ʙa suj Parvardigoras rohe ʙijoʙad»
Va ʙar On zindae, ki namemirad, tavakkal kun va ʙa sitoisi U tasʙeh guj va U xud ʙaroi ogohi az gunohoni ʙandagonas kofist
on, ki osmonhovu zamin va har ciro dar mijoni onhost, dar sas ruz ʙijofarid, on goh ʙa ars pardoxt. Ust Xudoi rahmon va dar ʙorai U az kase ʙipurs, ki ogoh ʙosad
Va cun ʙa onon gufta sud, ki Rahmonro sacda kuned, guftand: «Rahmon kist? Ojo ʙar har kas, ki tu farmon medihi, sacda kunem?» Va ʙar nafratason afzuda sud. (Sacda)
Buzurgu ʙuzurgvor ast on kase, ki dar osmon ʙurcho ʙijofarid va dar onho caroƣevu mohe toʙon padid ovard
Va Ust, ki saʙu ruzro ʙaroi kasone, ki mexohand iʙrat girand, jo sukrguzori kunand, az pai ham qaror dod
Bandagoni Xudoi rahmon kasone hastand, ki dar rui zamin ʙa furutani roh meravand. Va cun cohilon ononro xitoʙ kunand, ʙa muloimi suxan gujand
Va onon, ki saʙro dar sacda jo dar qijom ʙaroi Parvardigorason ruz mekunand
Va onon, ki megujand: «Ej Parvardigori mo, azoʙi cahannamro az mo ʙigardon, zero azoʙi cahannam azoʙest doim
Cahannam ʙad karorgohu ʙad makonest»
Va onon, ki cun nafaqa mekunand, isrof namekunand va xasisi namekunand, ʙalki mijoni in du rohi mijonaro megirand
Va onon, ki ʙo Xudoi jakto xudoi digare namegirand va kasero, ki Xudo kustanasro harom karda, ʙa ƣajri haq namekusand va zino namekunand. Va har ki in korho kunad, uquʙati gunohi xudro meʙinad
Azoʙas dar ruzi qijomat muzo'af (ducandon) mesavad va to aʙad ʙa xori dar on azoʙ xohad ʙud
ƣajri on kason, ki tavʙa kunand va imon ovarand va korhoi soista kunand. Xudo gunohonasonro ʙa nekiho muʙaddal mekunad va Xudo ʙaxsojandavu mehruʙon ast
Va har ki tavʙa kunad va kori soista kunad, ʙa soistagi nazdi Xudo ʙozgardad
Va onon, ki ʙa duruƣ sohidi namedihand va cun ʙar nopisandi ʙigzarand, ʙa sitoʙ az on duri mecujand
Va onon, ki cun ʙa ojoti Parvardigorason pandason dihand, dar ʙaroʙari on cun karonu kuron naʙosand
Va onon, ki megujand: «Ej Parvardigori mo, az hamsaronu farzandonamon dilhoi moro sod dor va moro pesvon! parhezgoron gardon!»
Inho hamon kasonand, ki ʙa xotiri saʙre, ki tahammul kardaand, ƣurfahoi ʙihistro muzd joʙand va dar on co ʙa durudu salomason ʙinavozand
Covidona dar on co ʙosand. Ci neku qarorgohu makonest
Bigu: «Agar du'o (vu iltico)-i sumo nameʙud, Parvardigori man ʙa sumo qadrdonie namekard. Dar haqiqat sumo duruƣ kardaed va cazoaton hamrohaton xohad ʙud»
To, sin, mim
Inhost ojoti in kitoʙi ravsan(-u fahmo)
Sojad az in, ki imon nameovarand, xudro halok sozi
Agar ʙixohem, az osmon ʙarojason mu'cizae nozil mekunem, ki dar ʙaroʙari on ʙa farmonʙari sar furud ovarand
Barojason har suxani tozae az Xudoi rahmon nozil savad, alʙatta az on rugardoni mekunand
Pas duruƣ ʙarovardand. Ba zudi xaʙari on cizhoe, ki masxaraas mekardand, ʙa onho ʙirasad
Ojo ʙa zamin nanigaristaand, ki ci qadar az har guna gijohoni neku dar on rujonidaem
Dar in iʙratest, vale ʙestarason mu'min naʙudaand
Ba rosti Parvardigori tu piruzmandu mehruʙon ast
Va Parvardigorat Musoro nido do, d, ki: ej Muso, ʙa sui on mardumi sitamgor ʙirav
qavmi Fir'avn. Ojo namexohand parhezgor savand
Guft: «Ej Parvardigori man, metarsam, ki duruƣgujam xonand
Va dili man tang gardad va zaʙonam kusoda nasavad. Horunro pajƣamʙari deh
Va ʙar man ʙa gunohe da'voe dorand, metarsam, ki maro ʙikusand»
Guft: «Hargiz, ojoti Maro har du nazdi onho ʙiʙared, Mo niz ʙo sumo hastem va guskunandaem
Pas nazdi Fir'avn raved va ʙigued: «Mo rasuli Parvardigori cahonijon hastem
ki ʙani-Isroilro ʙo mo ʙifiristi»
Guft: «Ojo ʙa hangomi kudaki nazdi xud parvarisat nadodem va tu cand sol az umratro dar mijoni mo naguzaronidi
Va on korro, ki az tu oar zad, nakardai? Pas tu kofiri ne'mati»
Guft: «On vaqt, ki cunon kardam, az xatokoron ʙudam
Va cun az sumo tarsidam, gurextam. Vale Parvardigori mam ʙa man pajomʙari dod va maro dar sumori pajomʙaron ovard
Va minnati in ne'matro ʙar man mekuni, ki ʙani-Isroilro ƣulom soxtai?»
Fir'avn guft: «Parvardigori cahonijon cist?»
Guft: «Agar ʙa jaqin mepazired, Parvardigori osmonhovu zamin va har ci mijoni onhost»
Ba onon, ki dar atrofas ʙudand, guft: «Ojo nasunided?»
Guft; «Parvardpgori sumo va Parvardigori padaroni avvalini sumo»
Fir'azn guft: «In pajomʙare, ki ʙar sumo firistoda suda, devona ast»
Guft: «Ust Parvardigori masriku maƣriʙ va har ci mijoni on dust, agar aql kuned»
Fir'avn guft: «Agar ʙa coi man kasi digarero ʙa xudoi giri, ʙa zindonat meafkanam»
Guft: «Hatto agar mu'cizae ravsan ʙaroi tu ovarda ʙosam?»
Guft; Agar rost megui, onro ʙijovar»
Asojasro partoft. Ba oskoro aƶdahoe sud
Va dastasro ʙerun ovard. Dar nazari ʙinandagon safed menamud
Ba ʙuzurgoni qavmas, ki kanoras ʙudand, guft: «In mard codugare donost
Mexohad ʙa codui. xud sumoro az sarzaminaton ʙerun kunad. Ci ra'j medihed?»
Guftand: «Az u va ʙa ʙarodaras muhlat ʙixoh va kason ʙa sahrho ʙifirist
to har codugari donoero, ki hajot, nazdi tu ʙijorand»
Codugaronro dar ruze mu'ajjan ʙa va'dagoh ovardand
Va mardumro guftand: «Ojo sumo niz cam' meoed
To agar codugaron piruz omadand, hama ʙa onho pajravi kunem!»
Cun codugaron omadand, ʙa Fir'avn guftand: «Ojo agar mo piruz savem, moro muzde xohad ʙud?»
Guft: «Ore, hama az nazdikonam xohed ʙud»
Muso ʙa onho guft: «Har ci mexohed, partoftan, ʙipartoed!»
Onon resmonhovu cuʙhoi xud ʙijafkandand va guftand: «Ba izzati Fir'avn, ki mo piruz sudem!»
Va Muso asojasro partoft. Nogoh hamai on duruƣhoero, ki soxta ʙudand, furu ʙurd
Codugaron ʙa sacda aftodand
Guftand: «Ba Parvardigori cahonijon imon ovardem
Parvardigori Muso va Horun!»
Guft: «Ojo pes az on, ki sumoro ruxsat diham, imon ovarded? Alʙatta on mard ʙuzurgi sumost, ki sumoro codu omuxtaast. Xohed did. Aknun dasthovu pohojatonro az capu rost xoham ʙurid va hamaatonro ʙar dor xoham kard!»
Guftand: «Boke nest, mo nazdi Parvardigoramon ʙozmegardem
Mo umed medorem, ki Parvardigoramon xatohoi moro ʙuʙaxsad, ki mo naxustin kasone hastem, ki imon ovardem»
Va ʙa Muso vahj kardem, ki saʙhangom ʙandagoni Maro ʙerun ʙiʙar, ki az pai sumo ʙijojand
Va Fir'avn cam'ovarandagoni sipohro ʙa sahrho firistod
ki inho guruhe andakand
va moro ʙa xasm ovardaand
va mo hamagi omodai cangem
Pas onhoro az ʙorhovu casmasorho ʙerun kardem
va az ganchovu xonahoi neku
ʙa in tarz hamaro ʙa ʙani-Isroil voguzostem
Fir'avnijon ʙa hangomi ʙaromadani oftoʙ az pai onho raftand
Cun on du guruh jakdigarro didand, joroni Muso guftand: «Giriftor omadem!»
Guft: «Hargiz, Parvardigori man ʙo man ast va maro roh xohad nison dod»
Pas ʙa Muso vahj kardem, ki asojatro ʙa darjo ʙizan. Darjo ʙisikoft va har pora cun kuhe azim gast
Va on guruhi digarro niz ʙa darjo rasonidem
Muso va hamai hamrohonasro nacot dodem
Va on digaronro ƣark soxtem
Alʙatta dar in iʙratest va ʙestarinason imon naovardand
Alʙatta Parvardigori tu piruzmandu ʙaxsanda ast
Va dostoni Iʙrohimro ʙarojason tilovat kun
On goh ki ʙa padaru qavmi xud guft: «Ci meparasted?»
Guftackd: «Butonero meparastem va muqimi ostonason hastem»
Guft: «Ojo vaqte onhoro mexoned, sadojatonro mesunavand
Jo ʙaroi sumo foidavu zijone dorand?»
Guftand: «Na, padaronamonro didaem, ki cunin mekardaand»
Guft: Ojo medoned, ki ci meparastidaed
sumo va padaronaton
Onho dusmanoni manand, vale Parvardigori cahonijon dusti man ast
On, ki maro ʙijofarida, sipas rohnamoijam mekunad
va on, ki ʙa man ta'om medihad va maro oʙ medihad
va cun ʙemor savam, sifojam meʙaxsad
va on, ki maro memironad va sipas zinda mekunad
va on, ki umed medoram, ki dar ruzi qijomat xatojamro ʙiʙaxsojad
Ej Parvardigori man, maro hikmat ʙaxs va maro ʙa soistagon ʙipajvand
Va zikri neki maro dar dahoni ojandagon andoz
va maro az vorisoni ʙihisti purne'mat qaror deh
va padaramro ʙijomurz, ki az gumrohon ast
va dar ruzi qijomat maro rasvo masoz
ruze, ki na mol naf' medihad va na farzandon
ƣajri on kas, ki ʙo qalʙe pokiza az sirk ʙa nazdi Xudo ʙijojad!»
Va ʙihistro ʙaroi parhezgoron nazdik orand
Va cahannamro dar nazari kofiron oskor kunand
Ba onho gujand: Cizhoe, ki ʙa coi Xudoi jakto meparastided, kucojand
Ojo joriaton mekunand, jo xud jori mecujand?»
Onho va kofironro sarmagun dar cahannam andozand
va hamai laskari Iʙlisro
Va dar hole, ki dar cahannam ʙo jakdigar husumat mekunandu, megujand
«Ba Xudo savgand, ki mo dar gumrohii oskor ʙudem
on goh ki sumoro ʙo Parvardigori cahonijon ʙaroʙar medonistem
Va moro ʙadkoron gumroh soxtand
va aknun moro safe'one (xaloskunandahoe) nest
va moro dusti mehruʙone nest
Kos ʙori digar ʙa dunjo ʙozgardem, to az mu'minon gardem»
Dar in iʙratest va ʙestarinason imon najovardand
Alʙatta Parvardigori tu ƣoliʙu mehruʙon ast
Qavmi Nuh pajomʙaronro duruƣ ʙarozardand
On goh ki ʙarodarason Nuh ʙa onho guft: «Ojo nametarsed
Man ʙaroi sumo pajomʙare rostgu hastam
Az Xudo ʙitarsed va ʙa man ito'at kuned
Man az sumo dar ʙaroʙari hidojati xud muzde nametalaʙam. Muzdi man tanho ʙar uhdai Parvardigori cahonijon ast
Pas az Xudo ʙitarsed va ʙa man ito'at kuned!»
Guftand: «Ojo ʙa tu imon ʙijovarem va hol on ki kamʙaƣalon pajravi tu hastand?»

Agar mefahmed, hisoʙas tanho ʙo Parvardigori man ast
Va man mu'minonro dur namekunam
Bimdihandae oskor hastam»
Guftand: «Ej Nuh agar ʙas nakuni, sangsor mesavi»

U va hamrohonasro dar on kistii pur nacot dodem

On goh, ki ʙarodarason Hud guft: «Ojo nametarsed

Az Xudo ʙitarsed va ʙa man ito'at kuned

Ojo ʙar sari har ʙalandi ʙa ʙehudagi ʙinoe ʙaland mesozed
Va ʙad-in pindor, ki hamesa zindaed, qasrxoe ʙino mekuned
Va har goh intiqom gired, cun ʙerahmon intiqom megired
Pas az Xudo ʙitarsed va az man ito'at kuned
Va ʙitarsed az on Xudoe, ki on ciro, ki medoned, ʙa sumo ato kardaast
Va ʙa sumo corpojonu farzandon ato kardaast
va ʙoƣhovu casmasoron
Man az azoʙi ruze ʙuzurg ʙar sumo ʙimnokam»

Inho cuz hamon duruƣu najrangi pesinijon nest
Va mo azoʙ naxohem sud»

Tu niz ʙasare monandi mo hasti. Agar rost megui, nisonae ʙijovar»

Onro kustand va pusajmon sudand

On goh ki Su'ajʙ ʙa onho guft: «Ojo az Xudo nametarsed

Alʙatta Parvardigori tu ƣoliʙu mehruʙon ast
Va in kitoʙ nozilsuda az coniʙi Parvardigori cahonijon ast
Onro ruhulamin nozil kardaast
ʙar dili tu, to az ʙimdihandagon ʙosi
ʙa zaʙoni araʙii ravsan
Va on dar navistahoi pesinijon niz hast
Ojo in nisona ʙar onho ʙasanda nest, ki ulamoi ʙani-Isroil az on ogohand
Agar onro ʙar jake az acamon (ƣajri araʙho) nozil karda ʙudem
va ʙarojason onro mexond, ʙa on imon nameovardand
Ba in tarz Qur'onro dar dilhoi gunahkoron roh dodem
Ba on imon nameovarand to azoʙi dardovarro ʙuʙinand
Va on azoʙ nogahon va ʙexaʙar ʙar onon furud meojad
Megujand: «Ojo moro muhlate xohand dod?»
Ojo ʙa azoʙi mo mesitoʙand
Didi, ki harcand solho ʙahramandason soxtem
ʙoz ham azoʙe, ki ʙa onho va'da suda ʙud, ʙar sarason omad
On ʙahramandiho ʙa holason naf' nakard
Mo hec dehaero halok nakardem, cuz on, ki ʙarojason ʙimdihandagone ʙudand
to pandason dihand. Zero mo sitamkor nestem
Va in Qur'onro sajtonho nozil nakardaand
Onon na loiqi in korand va na tavoni on dorand
Sajtonhoro az sunidani vahj dur dostaand
Pas ʙo Xudoi jakto xudoi digarero maxon, to maʙod dar sumori azoʙsavandagon daroi
Xesovandoni nazdikatro ʙitarson
Dar ʙaroʙari har jak az mu'minon, ki ʙa tu pajravi mekunad, xoksoru narm ʙos
Va agar ʙar tu nofarmoni kardand, ʙigu: «Man az korhoi sumo ʙezoram!»
Va ʙar Xudoi piruzmandu mehruʙon tavakkal kun
On, ki turo meʙinad, on goh, ki ʙarmexezi
va namoz xondanatro ʙo digar namozguzoron meʙinad
Alʙatta Ust sunavoi dono
Ojo sumoro ogoh kunam, ki sajtonho ʙa nazdi kiho meojand
Bar har duruƣgui gunahkor meojand
Gus medihand va ʙestarinason duruƣgujonand
Va gumrohon az pai soiron meravand
Ojo nadidai, ki soiron dar har vodie sargastaand
Va cizho megujand, ki xud amal namekunand
Ƣajri onho, ki imon ovardand va korhoi soista kardand va Xudoro farovon jod kardand va cun mavridi sitam voqe' sudand, intiqom giriftand. Va sitamkoron ʙa zudi xohand donist, ki ʙa ci makone ʙozmegardand
To, sin. In ast ojoti Qur'on va kitoʙi ravsangar
Rahnamun va xusxaʙarest ʙaroi mu'minon
onon, ki namoz meguzorand va zakot medihand va ʙa ruzi qijomat jaqin dorand
Amalhoi onhoero, ki ʙa oxirat imon nadorand, dar dar nazarason ʙijorostem. Az in ruj sargasta mondaand
Onho hamon kasonand, ki azoʙi saxt az oni onhost va dar oxirat zijonkortarand
Tu kase hasti, ki Qur'on az coniʙi Xudoi hakimu dono ʙa tu nozil mesavad
Muso ʙa xonavodai xud guft: «Man az dur otase didam, ʙa zudi, ki az on ʙarojaton xaʙare ʙijovaram jo porai otase. Sojad garm saved»
Cun ʙa otas rasid, sadojas dodand, ki ʙarakat doda suda on, ki daruni otas ast va on, ki dar kanori on ast. Va pok ast Xudoi jakto, on Parvardigori cahonijon
«Ej Muso, Man Xudoi ƣoliʙu hakim hastam
Asojatro ʙijafkan!»; Cun didas, ki monandi more mecunʙad, gurezon ʙozgast va ʙa aqiʙ nanigarist. «Ej Muso, matars. Pajomʙaron naʙojad, ki dar nazdi man ʙitarsand
ƣajri kase, ki gunohe karda ʙosad va pas az ʙadkori nekukor savad. Zero Man ʙaxsojandavu mehruʙonam
Dastatro dar gireʙon ʙiʙar, to ʙe hec oseʙe safed ʙerun ojad. Bo nuh nisona nazdi Fir'avn va qavmas ʙirav, ki mardume fosiqand»
Cun nisonahoi ravsani Moro didand, guftand: «In codue oskor ast!»
Bo on, ki dar dil ʙa on jaqin ovarda ʙudand, vale az rui sitamu ʙartaricui inkoras kardand. Pas ʙingar, ki oqiʙati taʙahkoron ci guna ʙuvad
Mo ʙa Dovudu Sulajmon donis dodem. Guftand: «Sukr Xudoro ast, ki moro ʙar ʙisjore az ʙandagoni mu'mini xud ʙartari dod!»
Va Sulajmon vorisi Dovud sud va guft: «Ej mardum, ʙa mo zaʙoni murƣon omuxtand va az har ne'mate ato kardand. Va in inojatest oskor!»
Sipohijoni Sulajmon az cinnu odami va parranda gird omadand va onho ʙa saf meraftand
To ʙa vodii murcagon rasidand. Murcae guft: «Ej murcagon, ʙa lonahoi xud daroed, to Sulajmonu laskarijonas sumoro ʙexaʙar pomol nakunand»
Sulajmon az suxani u laʙxand zadu guft: «Ej Parvardigori man, maro tavfiq deh to sukri ne'mati turo, ki ʙar man va padaru modari man arzoni dostai, ʙa coj ovaram va korhoi soistae kunam, ki tu xusnud savi va maro ʙa rahmati xud dar sumori ʙandagoni soistaat darovar!»
Dar mijoni murƣon custucu kard va guft: «Caro hudhudro nameʙinam. Ojo az ƣoiʙsudagon ast
Ba saxttarin tarze azoʙas mekunam jo sarasro meʙuram, agar ʙaroi man dalele ravsan naorad»
Der kardanas ʙa daroz nakasid. Bijomadu guft «Ba cize dast joftaam, ki tu dast najofta ʙudi va az Saʙo ʙarojat xaʙare durust ovardaam
Zanero joftam, ki ʙar onho podsohi mekunad. Az har ne'mate ʙarxurdor ast va taxte ʙuzurg dorad
Didam, ki xud va mardumas ʙa coi Xudoi jakto oftoʙro sacda mekunand. Va sajton amalhojasonro dar nazarason ʙijorostaast va az rohi Xudo gumrohason kardaast, cunon ki rui hidojat naxohand did
Caro Xudoero, ki nihoni osmonhovu zaminro oskor mekunad va har ciro pinhon medored jo oskor mesozed, medonad, sacda nakunand
Xudoi jakto, ki hec xudoe ƣajri U nest. Parvardigori arsi azim». (Sacda)
Guft: «Aknun ʙingarem, ki rost guftai jo dar sumori duruƣgujoni
In nomai maro ʙiʙar va ʙar onho afkan, sipas ʙa jak su sav va ʙingar, ki ci cavoʙ medihand»
Zan guft: «Ej ʙuzurgon, nomae giromi ʙa sui man partofta sud
Noma az Sulajmon ast va in ast: «Ba nomi Xudoi ʙaxsojandai mehruʙon»
«Bar man ʙartari macued va ʙa taslim nazdi man ʙijoed»
Zan guft: «Ej ʙuzurgon, dar kori man ra'j ʙidihed, ki to sumo hozir naʙosed, man hec korero hal natavonam kard»
Guftand: Mo qudratmandon va sohiʙoni cangi saxt hastem. Korho ʙa dasti tust. Bingar, ki ci farmon medihi»
Zan guft: «Podsohon cun ʙa dehae darojand, vajronas mekunand va azizonasro xor mesozand. Ore, cunin kunand
Man hadjae nazdason mefiristam va menigaram, ki qosidon ci cavoʙ meovarand»
Cun qosid nazdi Sulajmon omad, Sulajmon guft: «Ojo mexohed ʙa mol maro jori kuned? On ci Xudo ʙa man doda, az on ci ʙa sumo doda ʙehtar ast. Na, sumo ʙa hadjai xud sodmon hasted
Aknun ʙa nazdason ʙozgard. Laskare ʙar sarason mekasem, ki hargiz toqati onro nadosta ʙosand. Va ʙa xorivu zori az on co ʙerunason mekunem»
Guft: «Ej ʙuzurgon, kadom jak az sumo taxti uro, pes az on, ki ʙa taslim nazdi man ojad, ʙarojam meovared?»
Ifrite az mijoni cinho guft: «Man qaʙl az on, ki az cojat ʙarxezi, onro nazdi tu hozir mekunam, ki man ʙar in kor ham tavonojamu ham ʙovarinok»
Va on kas, ki az ilmi kitoʙ ʙahrae dost, guft: «Man, pes az on, ki casm ʙar ham zani, onro nazdi tu meovaram». Cun onro nazdi xud did, guft: «In ʙaxsisi Parvardigori man ast, to maro ʙijozmojad, ki sukrguzoram jo kofiri ne'mat. Pas har ki sukr gujad, ʙaroi xud guftaast va har ki nosukri kunad, Parvardigori man ʙenijozu karim ast»
Guft: «Taxtasro digargun kuned, ʙuʙinem onro ʙozmesinosad jo az onhost, ki ʙoznatavonand sinoxt»
Cun omad, guftandas: «Ojo taxti tu cunin ʙud?» Guft: «Gujo hamon ast. Va mo pes az in ogoh suda ʙudem va taslim ʙudaem»
Va uro az har ci ʙa coi Xudoi jakto meparastid, ʙozdost. Zero u dar zumrai kofiron ʙud
Guftandas: «Ba sahni qasr daroj!» Cun ʙididas, pindost, havzi pur az oʙ ast. Doman az soqhojas ʙargirift. Sulajmon guft: «In sahnest sof az sisa». Guft: «Ej Parvardigori man, man ʙar xud sitam kardaam va inak ʙo Sulajmon dar ʙaroʙari Parvardigori cahonijon taslim sudam»
Va ʙa qavmi Samud ʙarodarason Solehro firistodem, ki: Xudoi jaktoro ʙiparasted. Nogahon du guruh sudand va ʙo jakdigar ʙa xusumat ʙarxostand
Guft: «Ej qavmi man, caro pes az neki ʙar ʙadi mesitoʙed? Caro az Xudo ʙaxsois namexohed? Sojad ʙar sumo rahmat ovarad»
Guftand: «Mo turo va joronatro ʙa foli ʙad giriftaem». Guft: «Foli ʙadaton nazdi Xudost. Inak mardume fireʙxurda hasted!»
Dar sahr nuh mardi nosoleh ʙudand, ki dar on sarzamin fasod mekardand, na isloh
Guftand; «Ba Xudo savgand xured, ki u va kasonas ro saʙona mekusem. Va cun kase ʙa talaʙi xunas ʙarxezad, ʙiguem: «Mo ʙa hangomn halokati kasoni u on co naʙudaem va mo rostguftorem»
Va ƣofil ʙudand, ki agar onho hilae andesidaand, Mo niz hilae andesidaem
Bingar, ki oqiʙati makrason ci sud: Mo onho va qavmasonro ʙa tamomi halok kardem
On xonahoi onhost, ki ʙa cazoi zulme, ki mekardand, xoli aftodaast. Dar on donojonro iʙratest
Onhoero, ki imon ovarda ʙudand va parhezgor ʙudand, nacot dodem
Va Lutro ʙa jod or. On goh ki ʙa qavmi xud guft: «Korhoi zist mekuned, dar hole, ki xud ʙa zistii on ogohed
Caro az rui sahvat ʙa coi zanon ʙa mardon sahvat meroned? Sumo mardume nodon hasted!»
Cavoʙi qavmi u in ʙud, ki guftand: «Xonadoni Lutro az dehi xud ʙerun kuned. Onon da'voi poki mekunand» (Porai)
U va kasonas, ƣajri zanasro, nacot dodem. Cunon xostem, ki on zan az ʙozmondagon ʙosad
Borone ʙar onho ʙoronidem va ʙoroni tahdidsudagon ci ʙad ʙoronest
Bigu; «Sukr Ollohro va salom ʙar ʙandagoni intixoʙkardai U. Ojo Olloh ʙehtar ast jo on cizho, ki sariki U qaror medihand
Jo on kase, ki osmonhovu zaminro ofarid va az osmon ʙarojaton oʙ firistod va ʙo on ʙustonhoe xusmanzar rujonidem, ki sumoro tavoni rujonidani daraxte az on nest. Ojo ʙo vucudi Olloh xudoi digare hast? Na, onho mardume hastand az haq qacrav
Jo on ki zaminro oromgoh soxt va dar on rudho pajdo kard, kuhho va mijoni du dare mone'e qaror dod, Ojo ʙo vucudi Olloh xudoi digare hast? Na, ʙestarinason namedonand
Jo on ki darmondaro cun ʙixonadas, posux medihad va ranc az u dur mekunad va sumoro dar zamin conisini pesinijon mesozad. Ojo ʙo vucudi Olloh xudoi digare hast? Ci andak pand megired
Jo on ki sumoro dar torikihoi ʙijoʙonu darjo roh menamojad va on ki pes az ʙoroni rahmatas ʙodhoro ʙa muƶda mefiristad. Ojo ʙo vucudi Olloh xudoi digare hast? Olloh ʙolotar ast az har ci sariki U mesozand
Jo on ki maxluqotro meofarinad, sipas onhoro ʙozmegardonad va on, ki az osmonu zamin ʙa sumo ruzi medihad. Ojo ʙo vucudi Olloh xudoi digare hast? Bigu; Agar rost megued: daleli xud ʙijovared!»
Bigu: «Hec kas dar osmonhovu zamin ƣajʙro namedonad, magar Olloh. Va niz namedonand ci vaqt zinda mesavand!»
Dar ʙoʙi oxirat ʙa jaqin rasidand? Na! Hamcunon dar sak hastand, ʙalki mardume noʙinojand
Kofiron guftand: «Ci guna agar movu padaronamon xok sudem, moro az qaʙr ʙerun meovarand
Ba mo va padaronamon ham pes az in cunin va'dae doda ʙudand. Inho cize ƣajri afsonahoi pesinijon nest!»
Bigu: «Dar zamin sajr kuned va ʙingared, ki pojoni kori gunahkoron ci guna ʙudaast!»
Barojason anduhgin maʙos va az hilae, ki meandesand, tangdil masav
Megujand: «Agar rost megued, on va'dai qijomat ci vaqt xohad ʙud?»
Bigu: «Sojad ʙa'ze az on ci ʙa sitoʙ metalaʙed, nazdiki sumo ʙosad»
Va Parvardigori tu fazli xudro ʙar mardum ato mekunad, vale ʙestarinason sukr namegujand
Va Parvardigori tu medonad, ki ci cizro dar dil nihon kardaand va ci cizro oskor mesozand
Va dar osmonhovu zamin hec cizi maxfi nest, ki on dar kitoʙi muʙin naomada ʙosad
In Qur'on ʙisjore az cizhoero, ki ʙani-Isroil dar on ixtilof dorand, ʙarojason hikojat mekunad
Va ʙaroi mu'mimon hidojatu rahmat ast
Alʙatta Parvardigori tu ʙa ra'ji xud mijonason hukm xohad kard, ki U ƣoliʙu donost
Pas ʙa Xudo tavakkal kun, ki tu hamroh ʙo haqiqate ravsan hasti
Tu nametavoni murdagokro sunavo sozi va ovozi xudro ʙa gusi karone, ki az tu ruj megardonand. Birasoni
Tu nametavoni kuronro az gumrohijason roh namoi. Ovozi xudro tanho ʙa gusi kasone tavoni rasond, ki ʙa ojoti Mo imon ovardaand va musalmon hastand
Cun farmoni qijomat muqarrar gardad, ʙarojason cunʙandae az zamin ʙerun meovarem, ki ʙo onon suxan ʙigujad, ki in mardum ʙa ojoti Mo jaqin nameovardand
Ruze, ki az har millate guruhero az onon, ki ojoti Moro duruƣ meʙarovardand, cam' meovarem va ononro ʙa saf ʙironand
to cun ʙa mahsar ʙirasand, gujad: «Ojo sumo ojoti Maro duruƣ meʙarovarded va hol on, ki donisi sumo ʙa on ihota najofta ʙud? On ci kore ʙud, ki mekarded?»
Ba cazoi sitame, ki mekardand, hukmi azoʙ ʙar onho muqarrar savad, ʙe on, ki hec suxane ʙigujand
Ojo nameʙinand, ki saʙro padid ovardem, to dar on ʙijoromand va ruzro ravsani ʙaxsidem. Alʙatta dar in ʙaroi mu'minon iʙrathost
Ruze, ki dar sur damida savad va hamai kasone, ki dar osmonhovu zamin hastand, ƣajri on kas ki Xudo ʙixohad, ʙitarsand va hama xoru zalil ʙa sui U ravon savand
Va kuhhoro ʙini, pindori, ki ʙeconand, hol on, ki ʙa sur'ati aʙr meravand. Kori Xudovand, ast, ki har cizero ʙa kamol xalq kardaast. Alʙatta U ʙa har ci mekuned, ogoh ast
Har kas, ki kori neke kunad, ʙehtar az onro mukofot girad va nekukoron az vahsati on ruz dar amon ʙosand
Va ononro, ki korhoi ʙad mekunand, sarnagun dar otas andozand, ojo cuz muvofiqi korhoe, ki kardaed, cazo joʙed
Ba man farmon suda, ki Parvardigori in sahrro ʙiparastam. Sahre, ki Xudovande, ki hama ciz az oni Ust, hurmatas nihoda va amr sudaam, ki az musalmonon ʙosam
Va Qur'onro tilovat kunam. Pas har ki hidojat joft, ʙa naf'i xud hidojat joftaast va har ki gumroh sud, ʙigu: «Man ʙimdihandae hastam»
Va ʙigu: «Sukr Xudorost. Ojoti xudro ʙa sumo nison medihad, to onhoro ʙisinosed. Va Parvardigori tu az hec kore, ki mekuned, ʙexaʙar nest»
To, sin, mim
In ast ojathoi in kitoʙi ravsangar
Baroi onho, ki imon meovarand, dostoni rostini Muso va Fir'avnro ʙar tu mexonem
Fir'avn dar on sarzamin ʙartari cust va mardumasro firqa-firqa soxt. Firqaero xor medost va pisaronasonro mekust va zanonasonro zinda meguzost, ki u az fasodkoron ʙud
Va Mo ʙar on hastem, ki ʙar mustaz'afoni (za'ifoni) rui zamin ne'mat dihem va ononro pesvojon sozem va vorison gardonem
Va onhoro dar on sarzamin oʙruvu qudrat ʙaxsidem va ʙa Fir'avnu Homon va laskarijonason cizero, ki az on metarsidand, nison dihem
Va ʙa modari Muso vahj kardem, ki siras ʙideh va agar ʙar u ʙimnok sudi uro ʙa darjo ʙijandoz va matars va ƣamgin masav, uro ʙa tu ʙozmegardonem va dar sumori pajomʙaronas meovarem
Xonadoni Fir'avn uro joftand, to dusmanonason va saʙaʙi anduhason gardad, Fir'avn va Homon va laskarijonason xato mekardand
Zani Fir'avn guft: «In saʙaʙi sodmonii manu tust. Uro nakused, sojad ʙa mo naf'e ʙirasonad, jo uro ʙa farzandi girem». Va namedonistand, ki ci mekunand
Dili modari Muso tang sud. Va agar dilasro qavi nakarda ʙudem, to az mu'minon ʙosad, nazdik ʙud, ki on sirro fos sozad
Va ʙa xohari u guft: «Az pai u ʙirav». Va zan ʙe on ki onho fahmand, az dur dar u menigarist
Pistoni hamai dojagonro az pes ʙar u harom karda ʙudem. On zan guft: «Ojo mexohed sumoro ʙa xonavodae rohnamoi kunam, ki uro ʙarojaton nigoh dorand va nekxohas ʙosand?»
Pas uro nazdi modaras ʙargardonidem, to casmoni on zan ravsan gardad va ƣamgin naʙosad va ʙidonad, ki va'dai Xudo haq ast, vale ʙestarinason namedonand
Cun ʙa haddi ʙuluƣ rasid va ʙoquvvat sud, uro hikmatu donis dodem va nekukoronro cunii mukofot medihem
Bexaʙar az mardumi sahr ʙa sahr doxil sud. Du tanro did, ki ʙo ham cang mekunand. In jak az pajravonas ʙud va on jak az dusmanonas. On ki az pajravonas ʙud, ʙar ziddi on digar, ki az dusmanonas ʙud, az u jori xost. Muso muste ʙar u zad va uro kust. Guft: «In kori sajton ʙud. U ʙa oskoro dusmane gumrohkunanda ast»
Guft: «Ej Parvardigori man, man ʙa xud sitam kardam. Maro ʙiʙaxsoj». Va Xudojas ʙiʙaxsid. Zero ʙaxsojandavu mehruʙon ast
Guft: «Ej Parvardigori man, ʙa sukri ne'mate, ki ʙar man ato kardi, hargiz pustiʙoni gunahkoron naxoham sud!»
Digar ruz dar sahr tarson va casm ʙar rohi hodisa megardid. Marde, ki diruz az u madad xosta ʙud, ʙoz ham az u madad xost. Muso ʙa u guft: «Tu ʙa oskoro gumroh hasti!»
Cun xost mardero, ki dusmani har dui onho ʙud, ʙizanad, guft: «Ej Muso, ojo mexohi hamcunon ki diruz jakero kusti, maro niz ʙikusi? Tu mexohi, ki dar in sarzamin zolime ʙosi va namexohi, ki az muslihon ʙosi»
Marde az durdasti sahr davon omadu guft: «Ej Muso, sardoroni sahr dar ʙorai tu masvarat mekunand to ʙikusandat. Berun ʙirav. Man xajrxohi tu hastam!»
Tarsonu nigaron az sahr ʙerun sud. Guft: «Ej Parvardigori man, maro az sitamkoron nacot deh!»
Cun ʙa coniʙi Madjan ravon sud, guft: «Sojad Parvardigori man maro ʙa rohi rost rahʙari kunad»
Cun ʙa oʙi Madjan rasid, guruhe az mardumro did, ki corpojoni xudro oʙ medihand va pusti sarason du zanro did, ki gusfandoni xudro ʙozmeronand, Guft: «Sumo ci mekuned?» Guftand: «Mo oʙ namedihem, to on goh, ki cuponon ʙozgardand, ki padari mo pire ʙuzurgvor ast»
Gusfandonro oʙ dod. Sipas ʙa soja ʙozgastu guft: «Ej Parvardigori man, man ʙa on ne'mate, ki ʙarojam mefiristi, muhtocam»
Jake az on du zan, ki ʙa ozarm (sarm) roh meraft, nazdi u omad va guft: «Padaram turo mexonad, to muzdi oʙ dodanatro ʙidihad». Cun nazdi u omad va sarguzasti xud ʙiguft, guft: «Matars, ki tu az mardumi zolim nacot joftai»
Jake az on du guft: «Ej padar, uro mardikor gir, ki agar cunin kuni, ʙehtarin mardi nerumandi ʙovarinokest, ki mardikor kardai»
Guft: «Mexoham jake az in du duxtaramro zani tu kunam, ʙa sarti on, ki hast sol mardikori man ʙosi. Va agar dah solro purra kuni, xud xidmatest va man namexoham, ki turo ʙa masaqqat afkanam. Insoolloh, maro az solehon xohj joft»
Guft: «In ast pajmon mijoni manu tu. Har jak az du muddatro, ki tamom kunam, ʙar man sitame, naxohad raft va Xudo ʙar on ci meguem, vakil ast»
Cun Muso muddatro tamom kard va ʙo zanas ravon sud, az sui Tur otase did. Ba kasoni xud guft: «In co isted, Otase didam. Sojad az on xaʙare jo porai otase ʙijovaram, to garm saved»
Cun nazdi otas omad, az kanorai rosti vodi dar on sarzamini muʙorak az on daraxt sado doda sud, ki ej Muso, man Xudoi jakto, Parvardigori cahonijonam
Asojatro ʙiparto! Cun didas, ki monandi more mecunʙad, gurezon ʙozgast va ʙa aqiʙ nanigarist. «Ej Muso, pes oju matars. Tu dar amon hasti
Dasti xud ʙa gireʙon ʙiʙar to ʙerun ojad safed ʙe hec oseʙe. Va to az vahsat ʙijoromi, dasti xud dar ʙaƣal kun. In du az coniʙi Parvardigorat huccathoi tu ʙaroi Fir'avn va atrofijoni ust, ki onon mardume nofarmonand»
Guft: «Ej Parvardigori man, jake az onhoro kustaam va metarsam maro ʙikusand
Va ʙarodaram Horun ʙa zaʙon az man fasehtar ast. Uro ʙa madadi man ʙifirist, to maro tasdiq kunad, ki ʙimi on doram, ki duruƣgujam sumorand»
Guft: «Turo ʙo ʙarodarat qavidast xohem kard va ʙarojaton huccate qaror medihem. Ba saʙaʙi nisonahoe, ki sumoro dodaem, ʙa sumo dast naxohand joft. Sumo va pajravonaton ƣoliʙ xohed ʙud»
Cun Muso ojoti ravsani Moro nazdason ovard, guftand; «In coduest soxta, mo az nijogonamon cunin cizhoe nasunidaem»
Va Muso guft: «Parvardigori man ʙa on kase, ki az coniʙi U ʙa hidojat omadaast va oqiʙati pisandida dar on dunjo az oni ust, ogohtar ast. Zero sitamkoron rastagor (nacotjofta) namesavand!»
Fir'avn guft: «Ej camoat, man ʙaroi sumo xudoe ƣajri xud namesinosam. Ej Homon, ʙaroi man ocur (xist) ʙipaz va torame (gunʙade) ʙaland ʙisoz, sojad xudoi Musoro ʙuʙinam, ki duruƣgujas pindoram»
U va laskarhojas ʙa nohaq dar zamin sarkasi kardand va pindostand, ki ʙa nazdi mo ʙozgardonida namesavand
Pas u va laskarhojasro giriftem va ʙa darjo partoftem. Bingar, ki oqiʙati kori sitamkoron ci guna ʙud
Va ononro az on guna pesvojone soxtem, ki mardumro ʙa otas da'vat mekunand va dar ruzi qijomat kase joriason nakunad
Dar in dunjo az pajason la'nat ravona soxtem va dar ruzi qijomat az zistrujonand
Pas az on, ki mardumi ruzgori pesinro halok soxtem, ʙa Muso kitoʙ dodem, to mardumro iʙratu hidojat va rahmat ʙosad. Sojad pand girand
On goh ki ʙa Muso farmoni amri pajƣamʙariro vahj kardem, tu na dar coniʙi ƣarʙii Tur ʙudi va na az hoziron
Vale Mo az on pas naslhoero ʙijofaridem, ki umrason ʙa daroz kasid. Va tu dar mijoni mardumi Madjan muqim naʙudi, ki ojoti Moro ʙar onho ʙixoni. Vale Mo ʙudem, ki pajomʙarone mefiristodem
Tu dar kanori Tur naʙudi, on goh ki Musoro nido kardem. Vale in rahmatest az coniʙi Parvardigorat to mardumero, ki pes az tu ʙimdihandae nadostand, ʙim dihj. Bosad, ki pandpazir savand
To cun ʙa saʙaʙi amalhoe, ki kardaand, musiʙate ʙa onho rasad, nagujand: «Ej Parvardigori mo, caro pajomʙare ʙar mo nafiristodi, to az ojoti Tu pajravi kunem va az mu'minon ʙosem?»
Cun pajomʙari rostguj az coniʙi Mo ʙar onon firistoda sud, guftand: «Caro on ci ʙa Muso doda suda, ʙa u doda nasuda?» Ojo inho pes az in ʙa on ci ʙa Muso doda suda ʙud, kofir nasuda ʙudand? Va guftand, ki in har du, du codust monandi ham va mo ʙa hec jak imon nameovarem
Bigu: «Agar rost megued, az coniʙi Xudovand kitoʙe ʙijovared, ki az in du ʙehtar roh ʙinamojad, to man ham az on pajravi kunam!»
Pas agar icoʙatat nakardand, ʙidon, ki az pai havoi nafsi xud meravand va kist gumrohtar az on kas, ki ʙe on, ki rohnamoi az Xudo xohad, az pai havoi nafsi xud ravad? Zero Xudo mardumi zolimro hidojat namekunad
Barojason suxan dar suxan pajvastem, ʙosad, ki pandpazir gardand
Kasone, ki pes az in kitoʙ kitoʙason doda ʙudem, ʙa on imon meovarand
Va cun ʙar onon tilovat sud, guftand: «Ba on imon ovardem, Haqqest az coniʙi Parvardigori mo va mo pes az on taslim ʙudaem»
Inon ʙa saʙaʙi saʙre, ki kardaand, du ʙor podos doda savand. Inon ʙadiro ʙa neki dur mekunand va niz az on ci ruzijason dodaem, sadaqa mekunand
Va cun suxani ʙehudae ʙisnavand, az on rujgardoni kunand va gujand: «Kirdorhoi mo az oni mo va kirdorhoi sumo az oni sumo. Ba salomat ʙimoned. Mo xostori cohilon nestem!»
Tu har kasro, ki ʙixohi, hidojat namekuni. Xudost, ki har kiro ʙixohad, hidojat mekunad va U hidojatjoftagonro ʙehtar mesinosad
Guftand: «Agar az dini tu pajravi kunem, moro az sarzaminamon ʙarmekanand». Ojo onhoro dar harame amn coj na dodaem, ki hama guna mevaho dar on faroham mesavad va in rizqest az coniʙi Mo? Vale ʙestarinason namedonand
Ci ʙaso mardumi dehaero halok soxtem, ki az zindagii xud ducori sarmasti suda ʙudand va in xonahoi onhost, ki ʙa'd az onho andak zamone kas dar onho sukno (maskan) girift va Mo vorisi onho ʙudem
Parvardigori tu mardumi dehahoro halok nakard, to on goh, ki az xudason pajomʙare ʙar onho firistod va u ojoti Moro ʙar onho ʙixond. Va mo dehahoro noʙud kardaem, ʙa saʙaʙi on, ki mardumas sitamkor ʙudaand
Cizhoe, ki ʙa sumo doda sudaast, mato'est va oroisi in zindagii dunjavist. Hol on ki on ci nazdi Xudost, ʙehtaru mondanitar ast. Caro aqlatonro kor namefarmoed
Ojo on kas, ki uro va'dahoi nek dodaem va on va'dahoro xohad did, monandi kasest, ki uro az mato'i incahoni ʙahramand kardaem va dar ruzi qijomat ham az hozir karda sudagon ast
Va ruze, ki ononro nido medihad va megujad: «Sarikonero, ki ʙaroi Man mepindostaed, kucojand?»
Onon, ki hukm dar ʙoraason tahqiq suda megujand: «Ej Parvardigori mo, inho kasone, hastand, ki mo gumrohason kardem. Az on ru gumrohason kardem, ki xud gumroh ʙudem. Az onho ʙezori mecuem va ʙa tu megaravem. Inho moro nameparastidaand»
Va gufta savad: «Aknun ʙutonatonro farjod kuned». Farjod mekunand, vale ʙa onho cavoʙ namedihand. Va cun, azoʙro ʙuʙinand, orzu kunand, ki kos az hidojatjoftagon meʙudand
Va ruze, ki Xudo nidojason kunad va gujad: «Pajomʙaronro ci guna qaʙul karded?»
Dar in ruz xaʙarho ʙar onon pusida savad va az jakdigar niz natavonand pursid
Ammo on kas, ki tavʙa karda va imon ovarda va amali soleh ʙa coj ovarda, sojad, ki az nacotjoftagon ʙosad
Parvardigori tu har ciro, ki ʙixohad, meofarinad va meixtijorad. Vale onhoro tavoni ixtijor nest. Pok ast Xudo va az har ci ʙarojas sarik mesozand va ʙartar ast
Va Parvardigori tu har ciro, ki dar dil pinhon dostaand, jo oskor kardaand, medonad
Ust Xudoi jakto. Hec xudoe ƣajri U nest. Sano (sukr) xosi Ust, ci dar in cahon va ci dar cahoni digar. Va farmon farmoni Ust. Va hamagon ʙa U ʙozgardonda mesaved
Bigu: «Ci tasavvur mekuned, agar Olloh saʙatonro to ruzi qijomat tuloni sozad? Ƣajri U kadom xudost, ki sumoro ravsani medihad? Magar namesunaved?»
